000057 
000058 ADVENTURE I. A SCANDAL IN BOHEMIA
000059 
000060 I.
000061 
000062 To Sherlock Holmes she is always THE woman. I have seldom heard
000063 him mention her under any other name. In his eyes she eclipses
000064 and predominates the whole of her sex. It was not that he felt
000065 any emotion akin to love for Irene Adler. All emotions, and that
000066 one particularly, were abhorrent to his cold, precise but
000067 admirably balanced mind. He was, I take it, the most perfect
000068 reasoning and observing machine that the world has seen, but as a
000069 lover he would have placed himself in a false position. He never
000070 spoke of the softer passions, save with a gibe and a sneer. They
000071 were admirable things for the observer--excellent for drawing the
000072 veil from men's motives and actions. But for the trained reasoner
000073 to admit such intrusions into his own delicate and finely
000074 adjusted temperament was to introduce a distracting factor which
000075 might throw a doubt upon all his mental results. Grit in a
000076 sensitive instrument, or a crack in one of his own high-power
000077 lenses, would not be more disturbing than a strong emotion in a
000078 nature such as his. And yet there was but one woman to him, and
000079 that woman was the late Irene Adler, of dubious and questionable
000080 memory.
000081 
000082 I had seen little of Holmes lately. My marriage had drifted us
000083 away from each other. My own complete happiness, and the
000084 home-centred interests which rise up around the man who first
000085 finds himself master of his own establishment, were sufficient to
000086 absorb all my attention, while Holmes, who loathed every form of
000087 society with his whole Bohemian soul, remained in our lodgings in
000088 Baker Street, buried among his old books, and alternating from
000089 week to week between cocaine and ambition, the drowsiness of the
000090 drug, and the fierce energy of his own keen nature. He was still,
000091 as ever, deeply attracted by the study of crime, and occupied his
000092 immense faculties and extraordinary powers of observation in
000093 following out those clues, and clearing up those mysteries which
000094 had been abandoned as hopeless by the official police. From time
000095 to time I heard some vague account of his doings: of his summons
000096 to Odessa in the case of the Trepoff murder, of his clearing up
000097 of the singular tragedy of the Atkinson brothers at Trincomalee,
000098 and finally of the mission which he had accomplished so
000099 delicately and successfully for the reigning family of Holland.
000100 Beyond these signs of his activity, however, which I merely
000101 shared with all the readers of the daily press, I knew little of
000102 my former friend and companion.
000103 
000104 One night--it was on the twentieth of March, 1888--I was
000105 returning from a journey to a patient (for I had now returned to
000106 civil practice), when my way led me through Baker Street. As I
000107 passed the well-remembered door, which must always be associated
000108 in my mind with my wooing, and with the dark incidents of the
000109 Study in Scarlet, I was seized with a keen desire to see Holmes
000110 again, and to know how he was employing his extraordinary powers.
000111 His rooms were brilliantly lit, and, even as I looked up, I saw
000112 his tall, spare figure pass twice in a dark silhouette against
000113 the blind. He was pacing the room swiftly, eagerly, with his head
000114 sunk upon his chest and his hands clasped behind him. To me, who
000115 knew his every mood and habit, his attitude and manner told their
000116 own story. He was at work again. He had risen out of his
000117 drug-created dreams and was hot upon the scent of some new
000118 problem. I rang the bell and was shown up to the chamber which
000119 had formerly been in part my own.
000120 
000121 His manner was not effusive. It seldom was; but he was glad, I
000122 think, to see me. With hardly a word spoken, but with a kindly
000123 eye, he waved me to an armchair, threw across his case of cigars,
000124 and indicated a spirit case and a gasogene in the corner. Then he
000125 stood before the fire and looked me over in his singular
000126 introspective fashion.
000127 
000128 "Wedlock suits you," he remarked. "I think, Watson, that you have
000129 put on seven and a half pounds since I saw you."
000130 
000131 "Seven!" I answered.
000132 
000133 "Indeed, I should have thought a little more. Just a trifle more,
000134 I fancy, Watson. And in practice again, I observe. You did not
000135 tell me that you intended to go into harness."
000136 
000137 "Then, how do you know?"
000138 
000139 "I see it, I deduce it. How do I know that you have been getting
000140 yourself very wet lately, and that you have a most clumsy and
000141 careless servant girl?"
000142 
000143 "My dear Holmes," said I, "this is too much. You would certainly
000144 have been burned, had you lived a few centuries ago. It is true
000145 that I had a country walk on Thursday and came home in a dreadful
000146 mess, but as I have changed my clothes I can't imagine how you
000147 deduce it. As to Mary Jane, she is incorrigible, and my wife has
000148 given her notice, but there, again, I fail to see how you work it
000149 out."
000150 
000151 He chuckled to himself and rubbed his long, nervous hands
000152 together.
000153 
000154 "It is simplicity itself," said he; "my eyes tell me that on the
000155 inside of your left shoe, just where the firelight strikes it,
000156 the leather is scored by six almost parallel cuts. Obviously they
000157 have been caused by someone who has very carelessly scraped round
000158 the edges of the sole in order to remove crusted mud from it.
000159 Hence, you see, my double deduction that you had been out in vile
000160 weather, and that you had a particularly malignant boot-slitting
000161 specimen of the London slavey. As to your practice, if a
000162 gentleman walks into my rooms smelling of iodoform, with a black
000163 mark of nitrate of silver upon his right forefinger, and a bulge
000164 on the right side of his top-hat to show where he has secreted
000165 his stethoscope, I must be dull, indeed, if I do not pronounce
000166 him to be an active member of the medical profession."
000167 
000168 I could not help laughing at the ease with which he explained his
000169 process of deduction. "When I hear you give your reasons," I
000170 remarked, "the thing always appears to me to be so ridiculously
000171 simple that I could easily do it myself, though at each
000172 successive instance of your reasoning I am baffled until you
000173 explain your process. And yet I believe that my eyes are as good
000174 as yours."
000175 
000176 "Quite so," he answered, lighting a cigarette, and throwing
000177 himself down into an armchair. "You see, but you do not observe.
000178 The distinction is clear. For example, you have frequently seen
000179 the steps which lead up from the hall to this room."
000180 
000181 "Frequently."
000182 
000183 "How often?"
000184 
000185 "Well, some hundreds of times."
000186 
000187 "Then how many are there?"
000188 
000189 "How many? I don't know."
000190 
000191 "Quite so! You have not observed. And yet you have seen. That is
000192 just my point. Now, I know that there are seventeen steps,
000193 because I have both seen and observed. By-the-way, since you are
000194 interested in these little problems, and since you are good
000195 enough to chronicle one or two of my trifling experiences, you
000196 may be interested in this." He threw over a sheet of thick,
000197 pink-tinted note-paper which had been lying open upon the table.
000198 "It came by the last post," said he. "Read it aloud."
000199 
000200 The note was undated, and without either signature or address.
000201 
000202 "There will call upon you to-night, at a quarter to eight
000203 o'clock," it said, "a gentleman who desires to consult you upon a
000204 matter of the very deepest moment. Your recent services to one of
000205 the royal houses of Europe have shown that you are one who may
000206 safely be trusted with matters which are of an importance which
000207 can hardly be exaggerated. This account of you we have from all
000208 quarters received. Be in your chamber then at that hour, and do
000209 not take it amiss if your visitor wear a mask."
000210 
000211 "This is indeed a mystery," I remarked. "What do you imagine that
000212 it means?"
000213 
000214 "I have no data yet. It is a capital mistake to theorize before
000215 one has data. Insensibly one begins to twist facts to suit
000216 theories, instead of theories to suit facts. But the note itself.
000217 What do you deduce from it?"
000218 
000219 I carefully examined the writing, and the paper upon which it was
000220 written.
000221 
000222 "The man who wrote it was presumably well to do," I remarked,
000223 endeavouring to imitate my companion's processes. "Such paper
000224 could not be bought under half a crown a packet. It is peculiarly
000225 strong and stiff."
000226 
000227 "Peculiar--that is the very word," said Holmes. "It is not an
000228 English paper at all. Hold it up to the light."
000229 
000230 I did so, and saw a large "E" with a small "g," a "P," and a
000231 large "G" with a small "t" woven into the texture of the paper.
000232 
000233 "What do you make of that?" asked Holmes.
000234 
000235 "The name of the maker, no doubt; or his monogram, rather."
000236 
000237 "Not at all. The 'G' with the small 't' stands for
000238 'Gesellschaft,' which is the German for 'Company.' It is a
000239 customary contraction like our 'Co.' 'P,' of course, stands for
000240 'Papier.' Now for the 'Eg.' Let us glance at our Continental
000241 Gazetteer." He took down a heavy brown volume from his shelves.
000242 "Eglow, Eglonitz--here we are, Egria. It is in a German-speaking
000243 country--in Bohemia, not far from Carlsbad. 'Remarkable as being
000244 the scene of the death of Wallenstein, and for its numerous
000245 glass-factories and paper-mills.' Ha, ha, my boy, what do you
000246 make of that?" His eyes sparkled, and he sent up a great blue
000247 triumphant cloud from his cigarette.
000248 
000249 "The paper was made in Bohemia," I said.
000250 
000251 "Precisely. And the man who wrote the note is a German. Do you
000252 note the peculiar construction of the sentence--'This account of
000253 you we have from all quarters received.' A Frenchman or Russian
000254 could not have written that. It is the German who is so
000255 uncourteous to his verbs. It only remains, therefore, to discover
000256 what is wanted by this German who writes upon Bohemian paper and
000257 prefers wearing a mask to showing his face. And here he comes, if
000258 I am not mistaken, to resolve all our doubts."
000259 
000260 As he spoke there was the sharp sound of horses' hoofs and
000261 grating wheels against the curb, followed by a sharp pull at the
000262 bell. Holmes whistled.
000263 
000264 "A pair, by the sound," said he. "Yes," he continued, glancing
000265 out of the window. "A nice little brougham and a pair of
000266 beauties. A hundred and fifty guineas apiece. There's money in
000267 this case, Watson, if there is nothing else."
000268 
000269 "I think that I had better go, Holmes."
000270 
000271 "Not a bit, Doctor. Stay where you are. I am lost without my
000272 Boswell. And this promises to be interesting. It would be a pity
000273 to miss it."
000274 
000275 "But your client--"
000276 
000277 "Never mind him. I may want your help, and so may he. Here he
000278 comes. Sit down in that armchair, Doctor, and give us your best
000279 attention."
000280 
000281 A slow and heavy step, which had been heard upon the stairs and
000282 in the passage, paused immediately outside the door. Then there
000283 was a loud and authoritative tap.
000284 
000285 "Come in!" said Holmes.
000286 
000287 A man entered who could hardly have been less than six feet six
000288 inches in height, with the chest and limbs of a Hercules. His
000289 dress was rich with a richness which would, in England, be looked
000290 upon as akin to bad taste. Heavy bands of astrakhan were slashed
000291 across the sleeves and fronts of his double-breasted coat, while
000292 the deep blue cloak which was thrown over his shoulders was lined
000293 with flame-coloured silk and secured at the neck with a brooch
000294 which consisted of a single flaming beryl. Boots which extended
000295 halfway up his calves, and which were trimmed at the tops with
000296 rich brown fur, completed the impression of barbaric opulence
000297 which was suggested by his whole appearance. He carried a
000298 broad-brimmed hat in his hand, while he wore across the upper
000299 part of his face, extending down past the cheekbones, a black
000300 vizard mask, which he had apparently adjusted that very moment,
000301 for his hand was still raised to it as he entered. From the lower
000302 part of the face he appeared to be a man of strong character,
000303 with a thick, hanging lip, and a long, straight chin suggestive
000304 of resolution pushed to the length of obstinacy.
000305 
000306 "You had my note?" he asked with a deep harsh voice and a
000307 strongly marked German accent. "I told you that I would call." He
000308 looked from one to the other of us, as if uncertain which to
000309 address.
000310 
000311 "Pray take a seat," said Holmes. "This is my friend and
000312 colleague, Dr. Watson, who is occasionally good enough to help me
000313 in my cases. Whom have I the honour to address?"
000314 
000315 "You may address me as the Count Von Kramm, a Bohemian nobleman.
000316 I understand that this gentleman, your friend, is a man of honour
000317 and discretion, whom I may trust with a matter of the most
000318 extreme importance. If not, I should much prefer to communicate
000319 with you alone."
000320 
000321 I rose to go, but Holmes caught me by the wrist and pushed me
000322 back into my chair. "It is both, or none," said he. "You may say
000323 before this gentleman anything which you may say to me."
000324 
000325 The Count shrugged his broad shoulders. "Then I must begin," said
000326 he, "by binding you both to absolute secrecy for two years; at
000327 the end of that time the matter will be of no importance. At
000328 present it is not too much to say that it is of such weight it
000329 may have an influence upon European history."
000330 
000331 "I promise," said Holmes.
000332 
000333 "And I."
000334 
000335 "You will excuse this mask," continued our strange visitor. "The
000336 august person who employs me wishes his agent to be unknown to
000337 you, and I may confess at once that the title by which I have
000338 just called myself is not exactly my own."
000339 
000340 "I was aware of it," said Holmes dryly.
000341 
000342 "The circumstances are of great delicacy, and every precaution
000343 has to be taken to quench what might grow to be an immense
000344 scandal and seriously compromise one of the reigning families of
000345 Europe. To speak plainly, the matter implicates the great House
000346 of Ormstein, hereditary kings of Bohemia."
000347 
000348 "I was also aware of that," murmured Holmes, settling himself
000349 down in his armchair and closing his eyes.
000350 
000351 Our visitor glanced with some apparent surprise at the languid,
000352 lounging figure of the man who had been no doubt depicted to him
000353 as the most incisive reasoner and most energetic agent in Europe.
000354 Holmes slowly reopened his eyes and looked impatiently at his
000355 gigantic client.
000356 
000357 "If your Majesty would condescend to state your case," he
000358 remarked, "I should be better able to advise you."
000359 
000360 The man sprang from his chair and paced up and down the room in
000361 uncontrollable agitation. Then, with a gesture of desperation, he
000362 tore the mask from his face and hurled it upon the ground. "You
000363 are right," he cried; "I am the King. Why should I attempt to
000364 conceal it?"
000365 
000366 "Why, indeed?" murmured Holmes. "Your Majesty had not spoken
000367 before I was aware that I was addressing Wilhelm Gottsreich
000368 Sigismond von Ormstein, Grand Duke of Cassel-Felstein, and
000369 hereditary King of Bohemia."
000370 
000371 "But you can understand," said our strange visitor, sitting down
000372 once more and passing his hand over his high white forehead, "you
000373 can understand that I am not accustomed to doing such business in
000374 my own person. Yet the matter was so delicate that I could not
000375 confide it to an agent without putting myself in his power. I
000376 have come incognito from Prague for the purpose of consulting
000377 you."
000378 
000379 "Then, pray consult," said Holmes, shutting his eyes once more.
000380 
000381 "The facts are briefly these: Some five years ago, during a
000382 lengthy visit to Warsaw, I made the acquaintance of the well-known
000383 adventuress, Irene Adler. The name is no doubt familiar to you."
000384 
000385 "Kindly look her up in my index, Doctor," murmured Holmes without
000386 opening his eyes. For many years he had adopted a system of
000387 docketing all paragraphs concerning men and things, so that it
000388 was difficult to name a subject or a person on which he could not
000389 at once furnish information. In this case I found her biography
000390 sandwiched in between that of a Hebrew rabbi and that of a
000391 staff-commander who had written a monograph upon the deep-sea
000392 fishes.
000393 
000394 "Let me see!" said Holmes. "Hum! Born in New Jersey in the year
000395 1858. Contralto--hum! La Scala, hum! Prima donna Imperial Opera
000396 of Warsaw--yes! Retired from operatic stage--ha! Living in
000397 London--quite so! Your Majesty, as I understand, became entangled
000398 with this young person, wrote her some compromising letters, and
000399 is now desirous of getting those letters back."
000400 
000401 "Precisely so. But how--"
000402 
000403 "Was there a secret marriage?"
000404 
000405 "None."
000406 
000407 "No legal papers or certificates?"
000408 
000409 "None."
000410 
000411 "Then I fail to follow your Majesty. If this young person should
000412 produce her letters for blackmailing or other purposes, how is
000413 she to prove their authenticity?"
000414 
000415 "There is the writing."
000416 
000417 "Pooh, pooh! Forgery."
000418 
000419 "My private note-paper."
000420 
000421 "Stolen."
000422 
000423 "My own seal."
000424 
000425 "Imitated."
000426 
000427 "My photograph."
000428 
000429 "Bought."
000430 
000431 "We were both in the photograph."
000432 
000433 "Oh, dear! That is very bad! Your Majesty has indeed committed an
000434 indiscretion."
000435 
000436 "I was mad--insane."
000437 
000438 "You have compromised yourself seriously."
000439 
000440 "I was only Crown Prince then. I was young. I am but thirty now."
000441 
000442 "It must be recovered."
000443 
000444 "We have tried and failed."
000445 
000446 "Your Majesty must pay. It must be bought."
000447 
000448 "She will not sell."
000449 
000450 "Stolen, then."
000451 
000452 "Five attempts have been made. Twice burglars in my pay ransacked
000453 her house. Once we diverted her luggage when she travelled. Twice
000454 she has been waylaid. There has been no result."
000455 
000456 "No sign of it?"
000457 
000458 "Absolutely none."
000459 
000460 Holmes laughed. "It is quite a pretty little problem," said he.
000461 
000462 "But a very serious one to me," returned the King reproachfully.
000463 
000464 "Very, indeed. And what does she propose to do with the
000465 photograph?"
000466 
000467 "To ruin me."
000468 
000469 "But how?"
000470 
000471 "I am about to be married."
000472 
000473 "So I have heard."
000474 
000475 "To Clotilde Lothman von Saxe-Meningen, second daughter of the
000476 King of Scandinavia. You may know the strict principles of her
000477 family. She is herself the very soul of delicacy. A shadow of a
000478 doubt as to my conduct would bring the matter to an end."
000479 
000480 "And Irene Adler?"
000481 
000482 "Threatens to send them the photograph. And she will do it. I
000483 know that she will do it. You do not know her, but she has a soul
000484 of steel. She has the face of the most beautiful of women, and
000485 the mind of the most resolute of men. Rather than I should marry
000486 another woman, there are no lengths to which she would not
000487 go--none."
000488 
000489 "You are sure that she has not sent it yet?"
000490 
000491 "I am sure."
000492 
000493 "And why?"
000494 
000495 "Because she has said that she would send it on the day when the
000496 betrothal was publicly proclaimed. That will be next Monday."
000497 
000498 "Oh, then we have three days yet," said Holmes with a yawn. "That
000499 is very fortunate, as I have one or two matters of importance to
000500 look into just at present. Your Majesty will, of course, stay in
000501 London for the present?"
000502 
000503 "Certainly. You will find me at the Langham under the name of the
000504 Count Von Kramm."
000505 
000506 "Then I shall drop you a line to let you know how we progress."
000507 
000508 "Pray do so. I shall be all anxiety."
000509 
000510 "Then, as to money?"
000511 
000512 "You have carte blanche."
000513 
000514 "Absolutely?"
000515 
000516 "I tell you that I would give one of the provinces of my kingdom
000517 to have that photograph."
000518 
000519 "And for present expenses?"
000520 
000521 The King took a heavy chamois leather bag from under his cloak
000522 and laid it on the table.
000523 
000524 "There are three hundred pounds in gold and seven hundred in
000525 notes," he said.
000526 
000527 Holmes scribbled a receipt upon a sheet of his note-book and
000528 handed it to him.
000529 
000530 "And Mademoiselle's address?" he asked.
000531 
000532 "Is Briony Lodge, Serpentine Avenue, St. John's Wood."
000533 
000534 Holmes took a note of it. "One other question," said he. "Was the
000535 photograph a cabinet?"
000536 
000537 "It was."
000538 
000539 "Then, good-night, your Majesty, and I trust that we shall soon
000540 have some good news for you. And good-night, Watson," he added,
000541 as the wheels of the royal brougham rolled down the street. "If
000542 you will be good enough to call to-morrow afternoon at three
000543 o'clock I should like to chat this little matter over with you."
000544 
000545 
000546 II.
000547 
000548 At three o'clock precisely I was at Baker Street, but Holmes had
000549 not yet returned. The landlady informed me that he had left the
000550 house shortly after eight o'clock in the morning. I sat down
000551 beside the fire, however, with the intention of awaiting him,
000552 however long he might be. I was already deeply interested in his
000553 inquiry, for, though it was surrounded by none of the grim and
000554 strange features which were associated with the two crimes which
000555 I have already recorded, still, the nature of the case and the
000556 exalted station of his client gave it a character of its own.
000557 Indeed, apart from the nature of the investigation which my
000558 friend had on hand, there was something in his masterly grasp of
000559 a situation, and his keen, incisive reasoning, which made it a
000560 pleasure to me to study his system of work, and to follow the
000561 quick, subtle methods by which he disentangled the most
000562 inextricable mysteries. So accustomed was I to his invariable
000563 success that the very possibility of his failing had ceased to
000564 enter into my head.
000565 
000566 It was close upon four before the door opened, and a
000567 drunken-looking groom, ill-kempt and side-whiskered, with an
000568 inflamed face and disreputable clothes, walked into the room.
000569 Accustomed as I was to my friend's amazing powers in the use of
000570 disguises, I had to look three times before I was certain that it
000571 was indeed he. With a nod he vanished into the bedroom, whence he
000572 emerged in five minutes tweed-suited and respectable, as of old.
000573 Putting his hands into his pockets, he stretched out his legs in
000574 front of the fire and laughed heartily for some minutes.
000575 
000576 "Well, really!" he cried, and then he choked and laughed again
000577 until he was obliged to lie back, limp and helpless, in the
000578 chair.
000579 
000580 "What is it?"
000581 
000582 "It's quite too funny. I am sure you could never guess how I
000583 employed my morning, or what I ended by doing."
000584 
000585 "I can't imagine. I suppose that you have been watching the
000586 habits, and perhaps the house, of Miss Irene Adler."
000587 
000588 "Quite so; but the sequel was rather unusual. I will tell you,
000589 however. I left the house a little after eight o'clock this
000590 morning in the character of a groom out of work. There is a
000591 wonderful sympathy and freemasonry among horsey men. Be one of
000592 them, and you will know all that there is to know. I soon found
000593 Briony Lodge. It is a bijou villa, with a garden at the back, but
000594 built out in front right up to the road, two stories. Chubb lock
000595 to the door. Large sitting-room on the right side, well
000596 furnished, with long windows almost to the floor, and those
000597 preposterous English window fasteners which a child could open.
000598 Behind there was nothing remarkable, save that the passage window
000599 could be reached from the top of the coach-house. I walked round
000600 it and examined it closely from every point of view, but without
000601 noting anything else of interest.
000602 
000603 "I then lounged down the street and found, as I expected, that
000604 there was a mews in a lane which runs down by one wall of the
000605 garden. I lent the ostlers a hand in rubbing down their horses,
000606 and received in exchange twopence, a glass of half and half, two
000607 fills of shag tobacco, and as much information as I could desire
000608 about Miss Adler, to say nothing of half a dozen other people in
000609 the neighbourhood in whom I was not in the least interested, but
000610 whose biographies I was compelled to listen to."
000611 
000612 "And what of Irene Adler?" I asked.
000613 
000614 "Oh, she has turned all the men's heads down in that part. She is
000615 the daintiest thing under a bonnet on this planet. So say the
000616 Serpentine-mews, to a man. She lives quietly, sings at concerts,
000617 drives out at five every day, and returns at seven sharp for
000618 dinner. Seldom goes out at other times, except when she sings.
000619 Has only one male visitor, but a good deal of him. He is dark,
000620 handsome, and dashing, never calls less than once a day, and
000621 often twice. He is a Mr. Godfrey Norton, of the Inner Temple. See
000622 the advantages of a cabman as a confidant. They had driven him
000623 home a dozen times from Serpentine-mews, and knew all about him.
000624 When I had listened to all they had to tell, I began to walk up
000625 and down near Briony Lodge once more, and to think over my plan
000626 of campaign.
000627 
000628 "This Godfrey Norton was evidently an important factor in the
000629 matter. He was a lawyer. That sounded ominous. What was the
000630 relation between them, and what the object of his repeated
000631 visits? Was she his client, his friend, or his mistress? If the
000632 former, she had probably transferred the photograph to his
000633 keeping. If the latter, it was less likely. On the issue of this
000634 question depended whether I should continue my work at Briony
000635 Lodge, or turn my attention to the gentleman's chambers in the
000636 Temple. It was a delicate point, and it widened the field of my
000637 inquiry. I fear that I bore you with these details, but I have to
000638 let you see my little difficulties, if you are to understand the
000639 situation."
000640 
000641 "I am following you closely," I answered.
000642 
000643 "I was still balancing the matter in my mind when a hansom cab
000644 drove up to Briony Lodge, and a gentleman sprang out. He was a
000645 remarkably handsome man, dark, aquiline, and moustached--evidently
000646 the man of whom I had heard. He appeared to be in a
000647 great hurry, shouted to the cabman to wait, and brushed past the
000648 maid who opened the door with the air of a man who was thoroughly
000649 at home.
000650 
000651 "He was in the house about half an hour, and I could catch
000652 glimpses of him in the windows of the sitting-room, pacing up and
000653 down, talking excitedly, and waving his arms. Of her I could see
000654 nothing. Presently he emerged, looking even more flurried than
000655 before. As he stepped up to the cab, he pulled a gold watch from
000656 his pocket and looked at it earnestly, 'Drive like the devil,' he
000657 shouted, 'first to Gross & Hankey's in Regent Street, and then to
000658 the Church of St. Monica in the Edgeware Road. Half a guinea if
000659 you do it in twenty minutes!'
000660 
000661 "Away they went, and I was just wondering whether I should not do
000662 well to follow them when up the lane came a neat little landau,
000663 the coachman with his coat only half-buttoned, and his tie under
000664 his ear, while all the tags of his harness were sticking out of
000665 the buckles. It hadn't pulled up before she shot out of the hall
000666 door and into it. I only caught a glimpse of her at the moment,
000667 but she was a lovely woman, with a face that a man might die for.
000668 
000669 "'The Church of St. Monica, John,' she cried, 'and half a
000670 sovereign if you reach it in twenty minutes.'
000671 
000672 "This was quite too good to lose, Watson. I was just balancing
000673 whether I should run for it, or whether I should perch behind her
000674 landau when a cab came through the street. The driver looked
000675 twice at such a shabby fare, but I jumped in before he could
000676 object. 'The Church of St. Monica,' said I, 'and half a sovereign
000677 if you reach it in twenty minutes.' It was twenty-five minutes to
000678 twelve, and of course it was clear enough what was in the wind.
000679 
000680 "My cabby drove fast. I don't think I ever drove faster, but the
000681 others were there before us. The cab and the landau with their
000682 steaming horses were in front of the door when I arrived. I paid
000683 the man and hurried into the church. There was not a soul there
000684 save the two whom I had followed and a surpliced clergyman, who
000685 seemed to be expostulating with them. They were all three
000686 standing in a knot in front of the altar. I lounged up the side
000687 aisle like any other idler who has dropped into a church.
000688 Suddenly, to my surprise, the three at the altar faced round to
000689 me, and Godfrey Norton came running as hard as he could towards
000690 me.
000691 
000692 "'Thank God,' he cried. 'You'll do. Come! Come!'
000693 
000694 "'What then?' I asked.
000695 
000696 "'Come, man, come, only three minutes, or it won't be legal.'
000697 
000698 "I was half-dragged up to the altar, and before I knew where I was
000699 I found myself mumbling responses which were whispered in my ear,
000700 and vouching for things of which I knew nothing, and generally
000701 assisting in the secure tying up of Irene Adler, spinster, to
000702 Godfrey Norton, bachelor. It was all done in an instant, and
000703 there was the gentleman thanking me on the one side and the lady
000704 on the other, while the clergyman beamed on me in front. It was
000705 the most preposterous position in which I ever found myself in my
000706 life, and it was the thought of it that started me laughing just
000707 now. It seems that there had been some informality about their
000708 license, that the clergyman absolutely refused to marry them
000709 without a witness of some sort, and that my lucky appearance
000710 saved the bridegroom from having to sally out into the streets in
000711 search of a best man. The bride gave me a sovereign, and I mean
000712 to wear it on my watch-chain in memory of the occasion."
000713 
000714 "This is a very unexpected turn of affairs," said I; "and what
000715 then?"
000716 
000717 "Well, I found my plans very seriously menaced. It looked as if
000718 the pair might take an immediate departure, and so necessitate
000719 very prompt and energetic measures on my part. At the church
000720 door, however, they separated, he driving back to the Temple, and
000721 she to her own house. 'I shall drive out in the park at five as
000722 usual,' she said as she left him. I heard no more. They drove
000723 away in different directions, and I went off to make my own
000724 arrangements."
000725 
000726 "Which are?"
000727 
000728 "Some cold beef and a glass of beer," he answered, ringing the
000729 bell. "I have been too busy to think of food, and I am likely to
000730 be busier still this evening. By the way, Doctor, I shall want
000731 your co-operation."
000732 
000733 "I shall be delighted."
000734 
000735 "You don't mind breaking the law?"
000736 
000737 "Not in the least."
000738 
000739 "Nor running a chance of arrest?"
000740 
000741 "Not in a good cause."
000742 
000743 "Oh, the cause is excellent!"
000744 
000745 "Then I am your man."
000746 
000747 "I was sure that I might rely on you."
000748 
000749 "But what is it you wish?"
000750 
000751 "When Mrs. Turner has brought in the tray I will make it clear to
000752 you. Now," he said as he turned hungrily on the simple fare that
000753 our landlady had provided, "I must discuss it while I eat, for I
000754 have not much time. It is nearly five now. In two hours we must
000755 be on the scene of action. Miss Irene, or Madame, rather, returns
000756 from her drive at seven. We must be at Briony Lodge to meet her."
000757 
000758 "And what then?"
000759 
000760 "You must leave that to me. I have already arranged what is to
000761 occur. There is only one point on which I must insist. You must
000762 not interfere, come what may. You understand?"
000763 
000764 "I am to be neutral?"
000765 
000766 "To do nothing whatever. There will probably be some small
000767 unpleasantness. Do not join in it. It will end in my being
000768 conveyed into the house. Four or five minutes afterwards the
000769 sitting-room window will open. You are to station yourself close
000770 to that open window."
000771 
000772 "Yes."
000773 
000774 "You are to watch me, for I will be visible to you."
000775 
000776 "Yes."
000777 
000778 "And when I raise my hand--so--you will throw into the room what
000779 I give you to throw, and will, at the same time, raise the cry of
000780 fire. You quite follow me?"
000781 
000782 "Entirely."
000783 
000784 "It is nothing very formidable," he said, taking a long cigar-shaped
000785 roll from his pocket. "It is an ordinary plumber's smoke-rocket,
000786 fitted with a cap at either end to make it self-lighting.
000787 Your task is confined to that. When you raise your cry of fire,
000788 it will be taken up by quite a number of people. You may then
000789 walk to the end of the street, and I will rejoin you in ten
000790 minutes. I hope that I have made myself clear?"
000791 
000792 "I am to remain neutral, to get near the window, to watch you,
000793 and at the signal to throw in this object, then to raise the cry
000794 of fire, and to wait you at the corner of the street."
000795 
000796 "Precisely."
000797 
000798 "Then you may entirely rely on me."
000799 
000800 "That is excellent. I think, perhaps, it is almost time that I
000801 prepare for the new role I have to play."
000802 
000803 He disappeared into his bedroom and returned in a few minutes in
000804 the character of an amiable and simple-minded Nonconformist
000805 clergyman. His broad black hat, his baggy trousers, his white
000806 tie, his sympathetic smile, and general look of peering and
000807 benevolent curiosity were such as Mr. John Hare alone could have
000808 equalled. It was not merely that Holmes changed his costume. His
000809 expression, his manner, his very soul seemed to vary with every
000810 fresh part that he assumed. The stage lost a fine actor, even as
000811 science lost an acute reasoner, when he became a specialist in
000812 crime.
000813 
000814 It was a quarter past six when we left Baker Street, and it still
000815 wanted ten minutes to the hour when we found ourselves in
000816 Serpentine Avenue. It was already dusk, and the lamps were just
000817 being lighted as we paced up and down in front of Briony Lodge,
000818 waiting for the coming of its occupant. The house was just such
000819 as I had pictured it from Sherlock Holmes' succinct description,
000820 but the locality appeared to be less private than I expected. On
000821 the contrary, for a small street in a quiet neighbourhood, it was
000822 remarkably animated. There was a group of shabbily dressed men
000823 smoking and laughing in a corner, a scissors-grinder with his
000824 wheel, two guardsmen who were flirting with a nurse-girl, and
000825 several well-dressed young men who were lounging up and down with
000826 cigars in their mouths.
000827 
000828 "You see," remarked Holmes, as we paced to and fro in front of
000829 the house, "this marriage rather simplifies matters. The
000830 photograph becomes a double-edged weapon now. The chances are
000831 that she would be as averse to its being seen by Mr. Godfrey
000832 Norton, as our client is to its coming to the eyes of his
000833 princess. Now the question is, Where are we to find the
000834 photograph?"
000835 
000836 "Where, indeed?"
000837 
000838 "It is most unlikely that she carries it about with her. It is
000839 cabinet size. Too large for easy concealment about a woman's
000840 dress. She knows that the King is capable of having her waylaid
000841 and searched. Two attempts of the sort have already been made. We
000842 may take it, then, that she does not carry it about with her."
000843 
000844 "Where, then?"
000845 
000846 "Her banker or her lawyer. There is that double possibility. But
000847 I am inclined to think neither. Women are naturally secretive,
000848 and they like to do their own secreting. Why should she hand it
000849 over to anyone else? She could trust her own guardianship, but
000850 she could not tell what indirect or political influence might be
000851 brought to bear upon a business man. Besides, remember that she
000852 had resolved to use it within a few days. It must be where she
000853 can lay her hands upon it. It must be in her own house."
000854 
000855 "But it has twice been burgled."
000856 
000857 "Pshaw! They did not know how to look."
000858 
000859 "But how will you look?"
000860 
000861 "I will not look."
000862 
000863 "What then?"
000864 
000865 "I will get her to show me."
000866 
000867 "But she will refuse."
000868 
000869 "She will not be able to. But I hear the rumble of wheels. It is
000870 her carriage. Now carry out my orders to the letter."
000871 
000872 As he spoke the gleam of the side-lights of a carriage came round
000873 the curve of the avenue. It was a smart little landau which
000874 rattled up to the door of Briony Lodge. As it pulled up, one of
000875 the loafing men at the corner dashed forward to open the door in
000876 the hope of earning a copper, but was elbowed away by another
000877 loafer, who had rushed up with the same intention. A fierce
000878 quarrel broke out, which was increased by the two guardsmen, who
000879 took sides with one of the loungers, and by the scissors-grinder,
000880 who was equally hot upon the other side. A blow was struck, and
000881 in an instant the lady, who had stepped from her carriage, was
000882 the centre of a little knot of flushed and struggling men, who
000883 struck savagely at each other with their fists and sticks. Holmes
000884 dashed into the crowd to protect the lady; but just as he reached
000885 her he gave a cry and dropped to the ground, with the blood
000886 running freely down his face. At his fall the guardsmen took to
000887 their heels in one direction and the loungers in the other, while
000888 a number of better-dressed people, who had watched the scuffle
000889 without taking part in it, crowded in to help the lady and to
000890 attend to the injured man. Irene Adler, as I will still call her,
000891 had hurried up the steps; but she stood at the top with her
000892 superb figure outlined against the lights of the hall, looking
000893 back into the street.
000894 
000895 "Is the poor gentleman much hurt?" she asked.
000896 
000897 "He is dead," cried several voices.
000898 
000899 "No, no, there's life in him!" shouted another. "But he'll be
000900 gone before you can get him to hospital."
000901 
000902 "He's a brave fellow," said a woman. "They would have had the
000903 lady's purse and watch if it hadn't been for him. They were a
000904 gang, and a rough one, too. Ah, he's breathing now."
000905 
000906 "He can't lie in the street. May we bring him in, marm?"
000907 
000908 "Surely. Bring him into the sitting-room. There is a comfortable
000909 sofa. This way, please!"
000910 
000911 Slowly and solemnly he was borne into Briony Lodge and laid out
000912 in the principal room, while I still observed the proceedings
000913 from my post by the window. The lamps had been lit, but the
000914 blinds had not been drawn, so that I could see Holmes as he lay
000915 upon the couch. I do not know whether he was seized with
000916 compunction at that moment for the part he was playing, but I
000917 know that I never felt more heartily ashamed of myself in my life
000918 than when I saw the beautiful creature against whom I was
000919 conspiring, or the grace and kindliness with which she waited
000920 upon the injured man. And yet it would be the blackest treachery
000921 to Holmes to draw back now from the part which he had intrusted
000922 to me. I hardened my heart, and took the smoke-rocket from under
000923 my ulster. After all, I thought, we are not injuring her. We are
000924 but preventing her from injuring another.
000925 
000926 Holmes had sat up upon the couch, and I saw him motion like a man
000927 who is in need of air. A maid rushed across and threw open the
000928 window. At the same instant I saw him raise his hand and at the
000929 signal I tossed my rocket into the room with a cry of "Fire!" The
000930 word was no sooner out of my mouth than the whole crowd of
000931 spectators, well dressed and ill--gentlemen, ostlers, and
000932 servant-maids--joined in a general shriek of "Fire!" Thick clouds
000933 of smoke curled through the room and out at the open window. I
000934 caught a glimpse of rushing figures, and a moment later the voice
000935 of Holmes from within assuring them that it was a false alarm.
000936 Slipping through the shouting crowd I made my way to the corner
000937 of the street, and in ten minutes was rejoiced to find my
000938 friend's arm in mine, and to get away from the scene of uproar.
000939 He walked swiftly and in silence for some few minutes until we
000940 had turned down one of the quiet streets which lead towards the
000941 Edgeware Road.
000942 
000943 "You did it very nicely, Doctor," he remarked. "Nothing could
000944 have been better. It is all right."
000945 
000946 "You have the photograph?"
000947 
000948 "I know where it is."
000949 
000950 "And how did you find out?"
000951 
000952 "She showed me, as I told you she would."
000953 
000954 "I am still in the dark."
000955 
000956 "I do not wish to make a mystery," said he, laughing. "The matter
000957 was perfectly simple. You, of course, saw that everyone in the
000958 street was an accomplice. They were all engaged for the evening."
000959 
000960 "I guessed as much."
000961 
000962 "Then, when the row broke out, I had a little moist red paint in
000963 the palm of my hand. I rushed forward, fell down, clapped my hand
000964 to my face, and became a piteous spectacle. It is an old trick."
000965 
000966 "That also I could fathom."
000967 
000968 "Then they carried me in. She was bound to have me in. What else
000969 could she do? And into her sitting-room, which was the very room
000970 which I suspected. It lay between that and her bedroom, and I was
000971 determined to see which. They laid me on a couch, I motioned for
000972 air, they were compelled to open the window, and you had your
000973 chance."
000974 
000975 "How did that help you?"
000976 
000977 "It was all-important. When a woman thinks that her house is on
000978 fire, her instinct is at once to rush to the thing which she
000979 values most. It is a perfectly overpowering impulse, and I have
000980 more than once taken advantage of it. In the case of the
000981 Darlington substitution scandal it was of use to me, and also in
000982 the Arnsworth Castle business. A married woman grabs at her baby;
000983 an unmarried one reaches for her jewel-box. Now it was clear to
000984 me that our lady of to-day had nothing in the house more precious
000985 to her than what we are in quest of. She would rush to secure it.
000986 The alarm of fire was admirably done. The smoke and shouting were
000987 enough to shake nerves of steel. She responded beautifully. The
000988 photograph is in a recess behind a sliding panel just above the
000989 right bell-pull. She was there in an instant, and I caught a
000990 glimpse of it as she half-drew it out. When I cried out that it
000991 was a false alarm, she replaced it, glanced at the rocket, rushed
000992 from the room, and I have not seen her since. I rose, and, making
000993 my excuses, escaped from the house. I hesitated whether to
000994 attempt to secure the photograph at once; but the coachman had
000995 come in, and as he was watching me narrowly it seemed safer to
000996 wait. A little over-precipitance may ruin all."
000997 
000998 "And now?" I asked.
000999 
001000 "Our quest is practically finished. I shall call with the King
001001 to-morrow, and with you, if you care to come with us. We will be
001002 shown into the sitting-room to wait for the lady, but it is
001003 probable that when she comes she may find neither us nor the
001004 photograph. It might be a satisfaction to his Majesty to regain
001005 it with his own hands."
001006 
001007 "And when will you call?"
001008 
001009 "At eight in the morning. She will not be up, so that we shall
001010 have a clear field. Besides, we must be prompt, for this marriage
001011 may mean a complete change in her life and habits. I must wire to
001012 the King without delay."
001013 
001014 We had reached Baker Street and had stopped at the door. He was
001015 searching his pockets for the key when someone passing said:
001016 
001017 "Good-night, Mister Sherlock Holmes."
001018 
001019 There were several people on the pavement at the time, but the
001020 greeting appeared to come from a slim youth in an ulster who had
001021 hurried by.
001022 
001023 "I've heard that voice before," said Holmes, staring down the
001024 dimly lit street. "Now, I wonder who the deuce that could have
001025 been."
001026 
001027 
001028 III.
001029 
001030 I slept at Baker Street that night, and we were engaged upon our
001031 toast and coffee in the morning when the King of Bohemia rushed
001032 into the room.
001033 
001034 "You have really got it!" he cried, grasping Sherlock Holmes by
001035 either shoulder and looking eagerly into his face.
001036 
001037 "Not yet."
001038 
001039 "But you have hopes?"
001040 
001041 "I have hopes."
001042 
001043 "Then, come. I am all impatience to be gone."
001044 
001045 "We must have a cab."
001046 
001047 "No, my brougham is waiting."
001048 
001049 "Then that will simplify matters." We descended and started off
001050 once more for Briony Lodge.
001051 
001052 "Irene Adler is married," remarked Holmes.
001053 
001054 "Married! When?"
001055 
001056 "Yesterday."
001057 
001058 "But to whom?"
001059 
001060 "To an English lawyer named Norton."
001061 
001062 "But she could not love him."
001063 
001064 "I am in hopes that she does."
001065 
001066 "And why in hopes?"
001067 
001068 "Because it would spare your Majesty all fear of future
001069 annoyance. If the lady loves her husband, she does not love your
001070 Majesty. If she does not love your Majesty, there is no reason
001071 why she should interfere with your Majesty's plan."
001072 
001073 "It is true. And yet--Well! I wish she had been of my own
001074 station! What a queen she would have made!" He relapsed into a
001075 moody silence, which was not broken until we drew up in
001076 Serpentine Avenue.
001077 
001078 The door of Briony Lodge was open, and an elderly woman stood
001079 upon the steps. She watched us with a sardonic eye as we stepped
001080 from the brougham.
001081 
001082 "Mr. Sherlock Holmes, I believe?" said she.
001083 
001084 "I am Mr. Holmes," answered my companion, looking at her with a
001085 questioning and rather startled gaze.
001086 
001087 "Indeed! My mistress told me that you were likely to call. She
001088 left this morning with her husband by the 5:15 train from Charing
001089 Cross for the Continent."
001090 
001091 "What!" Sherlock Holmes staggered back, white with chagrin and
001092 surprise. "Do you mean that she has left England?"
001093 
001094 "Never to return."
001095 
001096 "And the papers?" asked the King hoarsely. "All is lost."
001097 
001098 "We shall see." He pushed past the servant and rushed into the
001099 drawing-room, followed by the King and myself. The furniture was
001100 scattered about in every direction, with dismantled shelves and
001101 open drawers, as if the lady had hurriedly ransacked them before
001102 her flight. Holmes rushed at the bell-pull, tore back a small
001103 sliding shutter, and, plunging in his hand, pulled out a
001104 photograph and a letter. The photograph was of Irene Adler
001105 herself in evening dress, the letter was superscribed to
001106 "Sherlock Holmes, Esq. To be left till called for." My friend
001107 tore it open and we all three read it together. It was dated at
001108 midnight of the preceding night and ran in this way:
001109 
001110 "MY DEAR MR. SHERLOCK HOLMES,--You really did it very well. You
001111 took me in completely. Until after the alarm of fire, I had not a
001112 suspicion. But then, when I found how I had betrayed myself, I
001113 began to think. I had been warned against you months ago. I had
001114 been told that if the King employed an agent it would certainly
001115 be you. And your address had been given me. Yet, with all this,
001116 you made me reveal what you wanted to know. Even after I became
001117 suspicious, I found it hard to think evil of such a dear, kind
001118 old clergyman. But, you know, I have been trained as an actress
001119 myself. Male costume is nothing new to me. I often take advantage
001120 of the freedom which it gives. I sent John, the coachman, to
001121 watch you, ran up stairs, got into my walking-clothes, as I call
001122 them, and came down just as you departed.
001123 
001124 "Well, I followed you to your door, and so made sure that I was
001125 really an object of interest to the celebrated Mr. Sherlock
001126 Holmes. Then I, rather imprudently, wished you good-night, and
001127 started for the Temple to see my husband.
001128 
001129 "We both thought the best resource was flight, when pursued by
001130 so formidable an antagonist; so you will find the nest empty when
001131 you call to-morrow. As to the photograph, your client may rest in
001132 peace. I love and am loved by a better man than he. The King may
001133 do what he will without hindrance from one whom he has cruelly
001134 wronged. I keep it only to safeguard myself, and to preserve a
001135 weapon which will always secure me from any steps which he might
001136 take in the future. I leave a photograph which he might care to
001137 possess; and I remain, dear Mr. Sherlock Holmes,
001138 
001139                                       "Very truly yours,
001140                                    "IRENE NORTON, ne ADLER."
001141 
001142 "What a woman--oh, what a woman!" cried the King of Bohemia, when
001143 we had all three read this epistle. "Did I not tell you how quick
001144 and resolute she was? Would she not have made an admirable queen?
001145 Is it not a pity that she was not on my level?"
001146 
001147 "From what I have seen of the lady she seems indeed to be on a
001148 very different level to your Majesty," said Holmes coldly. "I am
001149 sorry that I have not been able to bring your Majesty's business
001150 to a more successful conclusion."
001151 
001152 "On the contrary, my dear sir," cried the King; "nothing could be
001153 more successful. I know that her word is inviolate. The
001154 photograph is now as safe as if it were in the fire."
001155 
001156 "I am glad to hear your Majesty say so."
001157 
001158 "I am immensely indebted to you. Pray tell me in what way I can
001159 reward you. This ring--" He slipped an emerald snake ring from
001160 his finger and held it out upon the palm of his hand.
001161 
001162 "Your Majesty has something which I should value even more
001163 highly," said Holmes.
001164 
001165 "You have but to name it."
001166 
001167 "This photograph!"
001168 
001169 The King stared at him in amazement.
001170 
001171 "Irene's photograph!" he cried. "Certainly, if you wish it."
001172 
001173 "I thank your Majesty. Then there is no more to be done in the
001174 matter. I have the honour to wish you a very good-morning." He
001175 bowed, and, turning away without observing the hand which the
001176 King had stretched out to him, he set off in my company for his
001177 chambers.
001178 
001179 And that was how a great scandal threatened to affect the kingdom
001180 of Bohemia, and how the best plans of Mr. Sherlock Holmes were
001181 beaten by a woman's wit. He used to make merry over the
001182 cleverness of women, but I have not heard him do it of late. And
001183 when he speaks of Irene Adler, or when he refers to her
001184 photograph, it is always under the honourable title of the woman.
001185 
001186 
001187 
001188 ADVENTURE II. THE RED-HEADED LEAGUE
001189 
001190 I had called upon my friend, Mr. Sherlock Holmes, one day in the
001191 autumn of last year and found him in deep conversation with a
001192 very stout, florid-faced, elderly gentleman with fiery red hair.
001193 With an apology for my intrusion, I was about to withdraw when
001194 Holmes pulled me abruptly into the room and closed the door
001195 behind me.
001196 
001197 "You could not possibly have come at a better time, my dear
001198 Watson," he said cordially.
001199 
001200 "I was afraid that you were engaged."
001201 
001202 "So I am. Very much so."
001203 
001204 "Then I can wait in the next room."
001205 
001206 "Not at all. This gentleman, Mr. Wilson, has been my partner and
001207 helper in many of my most successful cases, and I have no
001208 doubt that he will be of the utmost use to me in yours also."
001209 
001210 The stout gentleman half rose from his chair and gave a bob of
001211 greeting, with a quick little questioning glance from his small
001212 fat-encircled eyes.
001213 
001214 "Try the settee," said Holmes, relapsing into his armchair and
001215 putting his fingertips together, as was his custom when in
001216 judicial moods. "I know, my dear Watson, that you share my love
001217 of all that is bizarre and outside the conventions and humdrum
001218 routine of everyday life. You have shown your relish for it by
001219 the enthusiasm which has prompted you to chronicle, and, if you
001220 will excuse my saying so, somewhat to embellish so many of my own
001221 little adventures."
001222 
001223 "Your cases have indeed been of the greatest interest to me," I
001224 observed.
001225 
001226 "You will remember that I remarked the other day, just before we
001227 went into the very simple problem presented by Miss Mary
001228 Sutherland, that for strange effects and extraordinary
001229 combinations we must go to life itself, which is always far more
001230 daring than any effort of the imagination."
001231 
001232 "A proposition which I took the liberty of doubting."
001233 
001234 "You did, Doctor, but none the less you must come round to my
001235 view, for otherwise I shall keep on piling fact upon fact on you
001236 until your reason breaks down under them and acknowledges me to
001237 be right. Now, Mr. Jabez Wilson here has been good enough to call
001238 upon me this morning, and to begin a narrative which promises to
001239 be one of the most singular which I have listened to for some
001240 time. You have heard me remark that the strangest and most unique
001241 things are very often connected not with the larger but with the
001242 smaller crimes, and occasionally, indeed, where there is room for
001243 doubt whether any positive crime has been committed. As far as I
001244 have heard it is impossible for me to say whether the present
001245 case is an instance of crime or not, but the course of events is
001246 certainly among the most singular that I have ever listened to.
001247 Perhaps, Mr. Wilson, you would have the great kindness to
001248 recommence your narrative. I ask you not merely because my friend
001249 Dr. Watson has not heard the opening part but also because the
001250 peculiar nature of the story makes me anxious to have every
001251 possible detail from your lips. As a rule, when I have heard some
001252 slight indication of the course of events, I am able to guide
001253 myself by the thousands of other similar cases which occur to my
001254 memory. In the present instance I am forced to admit that the
001255 facts are, to the best of my belief, unique."
001256 
001257 The portly client puffed out his chest with an appearance of some
001258 little pride and pulled a dirty and wrinkled newspaper from the
001259 inside pocket of his greatcoat. As he glanced down the
001260 advertisement column, with his head thrust forward and the paper
001261 flattened out upon his knee, I took a good look at the man and
001262 endeavoured, after the fashion of my companion, to read the
001263 indications which might be presented by his dress or appearance.
001264 
001265 I did not gain very much, however, by my inspection. Our visitor
001266 bore every mark of being an average commonplace British
001267 tradesman, obese, pompous, and slow. He wore rather baggy grey
001268 shepherd's check trousers, a not over-clean black frock-coat,
001269 unbuttoned in the front, and a drab waistcoat with a heavy brassy
001270 Albert chain, and a square pierced bit of metal dangling down as
001271 an ornament. A frayed top-hat and a faded brown overcoat with a
001272 wrinkled velvet collar lay upon a chair beside him. Altogether,
001273 look as I would, there was nothing remarkable about the man save
001274 his blazing red head, and the expression of extreme chagrin and
001275 discontent upon his features.
001276 
001277 Sherlock Holmes' quick eye took in my occupation, and he shook
001278 his head with a smile as he noticed my questioning glances.
001279 "Beyond the obvious facts that he has at some time done manual
001280 labour, that he takes snuff, that he is a Freemason, that he has
001281 been in China, and that he has done a considerable amount of
001282 writing lately, I can deduce nothing else."
001283 
001284 Mr. Jabez Wilson started up in his chair, with his forefinger
001285 upon the paper, but his eyes upon my companion.
001286 
001287 "How, in the name of good-fortune, did you know all that, Mr.
001288 Holmes?" he asked. "How did you know, for example, that I did
001289 manual labour. It's as true as gospel, for I began as a ship's
001290 carpenter."
001291 
001292 "Your hands, my dear sir. Your right hand is quite a size larger
001293 than your left. You have worked with it, and the muscles are more
001294 developed."
001295 
001296 "Well, the snuff, then, and the Freemasonry?"
001297 
001298 "I won't insult your intelligence by telling you how I read that,
001299 especially as, rather against the strict rules of your order, you
001300 use an arc-and-compass breastpin."
001301 
001302 "Ah, of course, I forgot that. But the writing?"
001303 
001304 "What else can be indicated by that right cuff so very shiny for
001305 five inches, and the left one with the smooth patch near the
001306 elbow where you rest it upon the desk?"
001307 
001308 "Well, but China?"
001309 
001310 "The fish that you have tattooed immediately above your right
001311 wrist could only have been done in China. I have made a small
001312 study of tattoo marks and have even contributed to the literature
001313 of the subject. That trick of staining the fishes' scales of a
001314 delicate pink is quite peculiar to China. When, in addition, I
001315 see a Chinese coin hanging from your watch-chain, the matter
001316 becomes even more simple."
001317 
001318 Mr. Jabez Wilson laughed heavily. "Well, I never!" said he. "I
001319 thought at first that you had done something clever, but I see
001320 that there was nothing in it, after all."
001321 
001322 "I begin to think, Watson," said Holmes, "that I make a mistake
001323 in explaining. 'Omne ignotum pro magnifico,' you know, and my
001324 poor little reputation, such as it is, will suffer shipwreck if I
001325 am so candid. Can you not find the advertisement, Mr. Wilson?"
001326 
001327 "Yes, I have got it now," he answered with his thick red finger
001328 planted halfway down the column. "Here it is. This is what began
001329 it all. You just read it for yourself, sir."
001330 
001331 I took the paper from him and read as follows:
001332 
001333 "TO THE RED-HEADED LEAGUE: On account of the bequest of the late
001334 Ezekiah Hopkins, of Lebanon, Pennsylvania, U. S. A., there is now
001335 another vacancy open which entitles a member of the League to a
001336 salary of 4 pounds a week for purely nominal services. All
001337 red-headed men who are sound in body and mind and above the age
001338 of twenty-one years, are eligible. Apply in person on Monday, at
001339 eleven o'clock, to Duncan Ross, at the offices of the League, 7
001340 Pope's Court, Fleet Street."
001341 
001342 "What on earth does this mean?" I ejaculated after I had twice
001343 read over the extraordinary announcement.
001344 
001345 Holmes chuckled and wriggled in his chair, as was his habit when
001346 in high spirits. "It is a little off the beaten track, isn't it?"
001347 said he. "And now, Mr. Wilson, off you go at scratch and tell us
001348 all about yourself, your household, and the effect which this
001349 advertisement had upon your fortunes. You will first make a note,
001350 Doctor, of the paper and the date."
001351 
001352 "It is The Morning Chronicle of April 27, 1890. Just two months
001353 ago."
001354 
001355 "Very good. Now, Mr. Wilson?"
001356 
001357 "Well, it is just as I have been telling you, Mr. Sherlock
001358 Holmes," said Jabez Wilson, mopping his forehead; "I have a small
001359 pawnbroker's business at Coburg Square, near the City. It's not a
001360 very large affair, and of late years it has not done more than
001361 just give me a living. I used to be able to keep two assistants,
001362 but now I only keep one; and I would have a job to pay him but
001363 that he is willing to come for half wages so as to learn the
001364 business."
001365 
001366 "What is the name of this obliging youth?" asked Sherlock Holmes.
001367 
001368 "His name is Vincent Spaulding, and he's not such a youth,
001369 either. It's hard to say his age. I should not wish a smarter
001370 assistant, Mr. Holmes; and I know very well that he could better
001371 himself and earn twice what I am able to give him. But, after
001372 all, if he is satisfied, why should I put ideas in his head?"
001373 
001374 "Why, indeed? You seem most fortunate in having an employ who
001375 comes under the full market price. It is not a common experience
001376 among employers in this age. I don't know that your assistant is
001377 not as remarkable as your advertisement."
001378 
001379 "Oh, he has his faults, too," said Mr. Wilson. "Never was such a
001380 fellow for photography. Snapping away with a camera when he ought
001381 to be improving his mind, and then diving down into the cellar
001382 like a rabbit into its hole to develop his pictures. That is his
001383 main fault, but on the whole he's a good worker. There's no vice
001384 in him."
001385 
001386 "He is still with you, I presume?"
001387 
001388 "Yes, sir. He and a girl of fourteen, who does a bit of simple
001389 cooking and keeps the place clean--that's all I have in the
001390 house, for I am a widower and never had any family. We live very
001391 quietly, sir, the three of us; and we keep a roof over our heads
001392 and pay our debts, if we do nothing more.
001393 
001394 "The first thing that put us out was that advertisement.
001395 Spaulding, he came down into the office just this day eight
001396 weeks, with this very paper in his hand, and he says:
001397 
001398 "'I wish to the Lord, Mr. Wilson, that I was a red-headed man.'
001399 
001400 "'Why that?' I asks.
001401 
001402 "'Why,' says he, 'here's another vacancy on the League of the
001403 Red-headed Men. It's worth quite a little fortune to any man who
001404 gets it, and I understand that there are more vacancies than
001405 there are men, so that the trustees are at their wits' end what
001406 to do with the money. If my hair would only change colour, here's
001407 a nice little crib all ready for me to step into.'
001408 
001409 "'Why, what is it, then?' I asked. You see, Mr. Holmes, I am a
001410 very stay-at-home man, and as my business came to me instead of
001411 my having to go to it, I was often weeks on end without putting
001412 my foot over the door-mat. In that way I didn't know much of what
001413 was going on outside, and I was always glad of a bit of news.
001414 
001415 "'Have you never heard of the League of the Red-headed Men?' he
001416 asked with his eyes open.
001417 
001418 "'Never.'
001419 
001420 "'Why, I wonder at that, for you are eligible yourself for one
001421 of the vacancies.'
001422 
001423 "'And what are they worth?' I asked.
001424 
001425 "'Oh, merely a couple of hundred a year, but the work is slight,
001426 and it need not interfere very much with one's other
001427 occupations.'
001428 
001429 "Well, you can easily think that that made me prick up my ears,
001430 for the business has not been over-good for some years, and an
001431 extra couple of hundred would have been very handy.
001432 
001433 "'Tell me all about it,' said I.
001434 
001435 "'Well,' said he, showing me the advertisement, 'you can see for
001436 yourself that the League has a vacancy, and there is the address
001437 where you should apply for particulars. As far as I can make out,
001438 the League was founded by an American millionaire, Ezekiah
001439 Hopkins, who was very peculiar in his ways. He was himself
001440 red-headed, and he had a great sympathy for all red-headed men;
001441 so when he died it was found that he had left his enormous
001442 fortune in the hands of trustees, with instructions to apply the
001443 interest to the providing of easy berths to men whose hair is of
001444 that colour. From all I hear it is splendid pay and very little to
001445 do.'
001446 
001447 "'But,' said I, 'there would be millions of red-headed men who
001448 would apply.'
001449 
001450 "'Not so many as you might think,' he answered. 'You see it is
001451 really confined to Londoners, and to grown men. This American had
001452 started from London when he was young, and he wanted to do the
001453 old town a good turn. Then, again, I have heard it is no use your
001454 applying if your hair is light red, or dark red, or anything but
001455 real bright, blazing, fiery red. Now, if you cared to apply, Mr.
001456 Wilson, you would just walk in; but perhaps it would hardly be
001457 worth your while to put yourself out of the way for the sake of a
001458 few hundred pounds.'
001459 
001460 "Now, it is a fact, gentlemen, as you may see for yourselves,
001461 that my hair is of a very full and rich tint, so that it seemed
001462 to me that if there was to be any competition in the matter I
001463 stood as good a chance as any man that I had ever met. Vincent
001464 Spaulding seemed to know so much about it that I thought he might
001465 prove useful, so I just ordered him to put up the shutters for
001466 the day and to come right away with me. He was very willing to
001467 have a holiday, so we shut the business up and started off for
001468 the address that was given us in the advertisement.
001469 
001470 "I never hope to see such a sight as that again, Mr. Holmes. From
001471 north, south, east, and west every man who had a shade of red in
001472 his hair had tramped into the city to answer the advertisement.
001473 Fleet Street was choked with red-headed folk, and Pope's Court
001474 looked like a coster's orange barrow. I should not have thought
001475 there were so many in the whole country as were brought together
001476 by that single advertisement. Every shade of colour they
001477 were--straw, lemon, orange, brick, Irish-setter, liver, clay;
001478 but, as Spaulding said, there were not many who had the real
001479 vivid flame-coloured tint. When I saw how many were waiting, I
001480 would have given it up in despair; but Spaulding would not hear
001481 of it. How he did it I could not imagine, but he pushed and
001482 pulled and butted until he got me through the crowd, and right up
001483 to the steps which led to the office. There was a double stream
001484 upon the stair, some going up in hope, and some coming back
001485 dejected; but we wedged in as well as we could and soon found
001486 ourselves in the office."
001487 
001488 "Your experience has been a most entertaining one," remarked
001489 Holmes as his client paused and refreshed his memory with a huge
001490 pinch of snuff. "Pray continue your very interesting statement."
001491 
001492 "There was nothing in the office but a couple of wooden chairs
001493 and a deal table, behind which sat a small man with a head that
001494 was even redder than mine. He said a few words to each candidate
001495 as he came up, and then he always managed to find some fault in
001496 them which would disqualify them. Getting a vacancy did not seem
001497 to be such a very easy matter, after all. However, when our turn
001498 came the little man was much more favourable to me than to any of
001499 the others, and he closed the door as we entered, so that he
001500 might have a private word with us.
001501 
001502 "'This is Mr. Jabez Wilson,' said my assistant, 'and he is
001503 willing to fill a vacancy in the League.'
001504 
001505 "'And he is admirably suited for it,' the other answered. 'He has
001506 every requirement. I cannot recall when I have seen anything so
001507 fine.' He took a step backward, cocked his head on one side, and
001508 gazed at my hair until I felt quite bashful. Then suddenly he
001509 plunged forward, wrung my hand, and congratulated me warmly on my
001510 success.
001511 
001512 "'It would be injustice to hesitate,' said he. 'You will,
001513 however, I am sure, excuse me for taking an obvious precaution.'
001514 With that he seized my hair in both his hands, and tugged until I
001515 yelled with the pain. 'There is water in your eyes,' said he as
001516 he released me. 'I perceive that all is as it should be. But we
001517 have to be careful, for we have twice been deceived by wigs and
001518 once by paint. I could tell you tales of cobbler's wax which
001519 would disgust you with human nature.' He stepped over to the
001520 window and shouted through it at the top of his voice that the
001521 vacancy was filled. A groan of disappointment came up from below,
001522 and the folk all trooped away in different directions until there
001523 was not a red-head to be seen except my own and that of the
001524 manager.
001525 
001526 "'My name,' said he, 'is Mr. Duncan Ross, and I am myself one of
001527 the pensioners upon the fund left by our noble benefactor. Are
001528 you a married man, Mr. Wilson? Have you a family?'
001529 
001530 "I answered that I had not.
001531 
001532 "His face fell immediately.
001533 
001534 "'Dear me!' he said gravely, 'that is very serious indeed! I am
001535 sorry to hear you say that. The fund was, of course, for the
001536 propagation and spread of the red-heads as well as for their
001537 maintenance. It is exceedingly unfortunate that you should be a
001538 bachelor.'
001539 
001540 "My face lengthened at this, Mr. Holmes, for I thought that I was
001541 not to have the vacancy after all; but after thinking it over for
001542 a few minutes he said that it would be all right.
001543 
001544 "'In the case of another,' said he, 'the objection might be
001545 fatal, but we must stretch a point in favour of a man with such a
001546 head of hair as yours. When shall you be able to enter upon your
001547 new duties?'
001548 
001549 "'Well, it is a little awkward, for I have a business already,'
001550 said I.
001551 
001552 "'Oh, never mind about that, Mr. Wilson!' said Vincent Spaulding.
001553 'I should be able to look after that for you.'
001554 
001555 "'What would be the hours?' I asked.
001556 
001557 "'Ten to two.'
001558 
001559 "Now a pawnbroker's business is mostly done of an evening, Mr.
001560 Holmes, especially Thursday and Friday evening, which is just
001561 before pay-day; so it would suit me very well to earn a little in
001562 the mornings. Besides, I knew that my assistant was a good man,
001563 and that he would see to anything that turned up.
001564 
001565 "'That would suit me very well,' said I. 'And the pay?'
001566 
001567 "'Is 4 pounds a week.'
001568 
001569 "'And the work?'
001570 
001571 "'Is purely nominal.'
001572 
001573 "'What do you call purely nominal?'
001574 
001575 "'Well, you have to be in the office, or at least in the
001576 building, the whole time. If you leave, you forfeit your whole
001577 position forever. The will is very clear upon that point. You
001578 don't comply with the conditions if you budge from the office
001579 during that time.'
001580 
001581 "'It's only four hours a day, and I should not think of leaving,'
001582 said I.
001583 
001584 "'No excuse will avail,' said Mr. Duncan Ross; 'neither sickness
001585 nor business nor anything else. There you must stay, or you lose
001586 your billet.'
001587 
001588 "'And the work?'
001589 
001590 "'Is to copy out the "Encyclopaedia Britannica." There is the first
001591 volume of it in that press. You must find your own ink, pens, and
001592 blotting-paper, but we provide this table and chair. Will you be
001593 ready to-morrow?'
001594 
001595 "'Certainly,' I answered.
001596 
001597 "'Then, good-bye, Mr. Jabez Wilson, and let me congratulate you
001598 once more on the important position which you have been fortunate
001599 enough to gain.' He bowed me out of the room and I went home with
001600 my assistant, hardly knowing what to say or do, I was so pleased
001601 at my own good fortune.
001602 
001603 "Well, I thought over the matter all day, and by evening I was in
001604 low spirits again; for I had quite persuaded myself that the
001605 whole affair must be some great hoax or fraud, though what its
001606 object might be I could not imagine. It seemed altogether past
001607 belief that anyone could make such a will, or that they would pay
001608 such a sum for doing anything so simple as copying out the
001609 'Encyclopaedia Britannica.' Vincent Spaulding did what he could to
001610 cheer me up, but by bedtime I had reasoned myself out of the
001611 whole thing. However, in the morning I determined to have a look
001612 at it anyhow, so I bought a penny bottle of ink, and with a
001613 quill-pen, and seven sheets of foolscap paper, I started off for
001614 Pope's Court.
001615 
001616 "Well, to my surprise and delight, everything was as right as
001617 possible. The table was set out ready for me, and Mr. Duncan Ross
001618 was there to see that I got fairly to work. He started me off
001619 upon the letter A, and then he left me; but he would drop in from
001620 time to time to see that all was right with me. At two o'clock he
001621 bade me good-day, complimented me upon the amount that I had
001622 written, and locked the door of the office after me.
001623 
001624 "This went on day after day, Mr. Holmes, and on Saturday the
001625 manager came in and planked down four golden sovereigns for my
001626 week's work. It was the same next week, and the same the week
001627 after. Every morning I was there at ten, and every afternoon I
001628 left at two. By degrees Mr. Duncan Ross took to coming in only
001629 once of a morning, and then, after a time, he did not come in at
001630 all. Still, of course, I never dared to leave the room for an
001631 instant, for I was not sure when he might come, and the billet
001632 was such a good one, and suited me so well, that I would not risk
001633 the loss of it.
001634 
001635 "Eight weeks passed away like this, and I had written about
001636 Abbots and Archery and Armour and Architecture and Attica, and
001637 hoped with diligence that I might get on to the B's before very
001638 long. It cost me something in foolscap, and I had pretty nearly
001639 filled a shelf with my writings. And then suddenly the whole
001640 business came to an end."
001641 
001642 "To an end?"
001643 
001644 "Yes, sir. And no later than this morning. I went to my work as
001645 usual at ten o'clock, but the door was shut and locked, with a
001646 little square of cardboard hammered on to the middle of the
001647 panel with a tack. Here it is, and you can read for yourself."
001648 
001649 He held up a piece of white cardboard about the size of a sheet
001650 of note-paper. It read in this fashion:
001651 
001652                   THE RED-HEADED LEAGUE
001653 
001654                            IS
001655 
001656                         DISSOLVED.
001657 
001658                      October 9, 1890.
001659 
001660 Sherlock Holmes and I surveyed this curt announcement and the
001661 rueful face behind it, until the comical side of the affair so
001662 completely overtopped every other consideration that we both
001663 burst out into a roar of laughter.
001664 
001665 "I cannot see that there is anything very funny," cried our
001666 client, flushing up to the roots of his flaming head. "If you can
001667 do nothing better than laugh at me, I can go elsewhere."
001668 
001669 "No, no," cried Holmes, shoving him back into the chair from
001670 which he had half risen. "I really wouldn't miss your case for
001671 the world. It is most refreshingly unusual. But there is, if you
001672 will excuse my saying so, something just a little funny about it.
001673 Pray what steps did you take when you found the card upon the
001674 door?"
001675 
001676 "I was staggered, sir. I did not know what to do. Then I called
001677 at the offices round, but none of them seemed to know anything
001678 about it. Finally, I went to the landlord, who is an accountant
001679 living on the ground-floor, and I asked him if he could tell me
001680 what had become of the Red-headed League. He said that he had
001681 never heard of any such body. Then I asked him who Mr. Duncan
001682 Ross was. He answered that the name was new to him.
001683 
001684 "'Well,' said I, 'the gentleman at No. 4.'
001685
