003192 Boscombe Pool, which is a small lake formed by the spreading out
003193 of the stream which runs down the Boscombe Valley. He had been
003194 out with his serving-man in the morning at Ross, and he had told
003195 the man that he must hurry, as he had an appointment of
003196 importance to keep at three. From that appointment he never came
003197 back alive.
003198 
003199 "From Hatherley Farm-house to the Boscombe Pool is a quarter of a
003200 mile, and two people saw him as he passed over this ground. One
003201 was an old woman, whose name is not mentioned, and the other was
003202 William Crowder, a game-keeper in the employ of Mr. Turner. Both
003203 these witnesses depose that Mr. McCarthy was walking alone. The
003204 game-keeper adds that within a few minutes of his seeing Mr.
003205 McCarthy pass he had seen his son, Mr. James McCarthy, going the
003206 same way with a gun under his arm. To the best of his belief, the
003207 father was actually in sight at the time, and the son was
003208 following him. He thought no more of the matter until he heard in
003209 the evening of the tragedy that had occurred.
003210 
003211 "The two McCarthys were seen after the time when William Crowder,
003212 the game-keeper, lost sight of them. The Boscombe Pool is thickly
003213 wooded round, with just a fringe of grass and of reeds round the
003214 edge. A girl of fourteen, Patience Moran, who is the daughter of
003215 the lodge-keeper of the Boscombe Valley estate, was in one of the
003216 woods picking flowers. She states that while she was there she
003217 saw, at the border of the wood and close by the lake, Mr.
003218 McCarthy and his son, and that they appeared to be having a
003219 violent quarrel. She heard Mr. McCarthy the elder using very
003220 strong language to his son, and she saw the latter raise up his
003221 hand as if to strike his father. She was so frightened by their
003222 violence that she ran away and told her mother when she reached
003223 home that she had left the two McCarthys quarrelling near
003224 Boscombe Pool, and that she was afraid that they were going to
003225 fight. She had hardly said the words when young Mr. McCarthy came
003226 running up to the lodge to say that he had found his father dead
003227 in the wood, and to ask for the help of the lodge-keeper. He was
003228 much excited, without either his gun or his hat, and his right
003229 hand and sleeve were observed to be stained with fresh blood. On
003230 following him they found the dead body stretched out upon the
003231 grass beside the pool. The head had been beaten in by repeated
003232 blows of some heavy and blunt weapon. The injuries were such as
003233 might very well have been inflicted by the butt-end of his son's
003234 gun, which was found lying on the grass within a few paces of the
003235 body. Under these circumstances the young man was instantly
003236 arrested, and a verdict of 'wilful murder' having been returned
003237 at the inquest on Tuesday, he was on Wednesday brought before the
003238 magistrates at Ross, who have referred the case to the next
003239 Assizes. Those are the main facts of the case as they came out
003240 before the coroner and the police-court."
003241 
003242 "I could hardly imagine a more damning case," I remarked. "If
003243 ever circumstantial evidence pointed to a criminal it does so
003244 here."
003245 
003246 "Circumstantial evidence is a very tricky thing," answered Holmes
003247 thoughtfully. "It may seem to point very straight to one thing,
003248 but if you shift your own point of view a little, you may find it
003249 pointing in an equally uncompromising manner to something
003250 entirely different. It must be confessed, however, that the case
003251 looks exceedingly grave against the young man, and it is very
003252 possible that he is indeed the culprit. There are several people
003253 in the neighbourhood, however, and among them Miss Turner, the
003254 daughter of the neighbouring landowner, who believe in his
003255 innocence, and who have retained Lestrade, whom you may recollect
003256 in connection with the Study in Scarlet, to work out the case in
003257 his interest. Lestrade, being rather puzzled, has referred the
003258 case to me, and hence it is that two middle-aged gentlemen are
003259 flying westward at fifty miles an hour instead of quietly
003260 digesting their breakfasts at home."
003261 
003262 "I am afraid," said I, "that the facts are so obvious that you
003263 will find little credit to be gained out of this case."
003264 
003265 "There is nothing more deceptive than an obvious fact," he
003266 answered, laughing. "Besides, we may chance to hit upon some
003267 other obvious facts which may have been by no means obvious to
003268 Mr. Lestrade. You know me too well to think that I am boasting
003269 when I say that I shall either confirm or destroy his theory by
003270 means which he is quite incapable of employing, or even of
003271 understanding. To take the first example to hand, I very clearly
003272 perceive that in your bedroom the window is upon the right-hand
003273 side, and yet I question whether Mr. Lestrade would have noted
003274 even so self-evident a thing as that."
003275 
003276 "How on earth--"
003277 
003278 "My dear fellow, I know you well. I know the military neatness
003279 which characterises you. You shave every morning, and in this
003280 season you shave by the sunlight; but since your shaving is less
003281 and less complete as we get farther back on the left side, until
003282 it becomes positively slovenly as we get round the angle of the
003283 jaw, it is surely very clear that that side is less illuminated
003284 than the other. I could not imagine a man of your habits looking
003285 at himself in an equal light and being satisfied with such a
003286 result. I only quote this as a trivial example of observation and
003287 inference. Therein lies my mtier, and it is just possible that
003288 it may be of some service in the investigation which lies before
003289 us. There are one or two minor points which were brought out in
003290 the inquest, and which are worth considering."
003291 
003292 "What are they?"
003293 
003294 "It appears that his arrest did not take place at once, but after
003295 the return to Hatherley Farm. On the inspector of constabulary
003296 informing him that he was a prisoner, he remarked that he was not
003297 surprised to hear it, and that it was no more than his deserts.
003298 This observation of his had the natural effect of removing any
003299 traces of doubt which might have remained in the minds of the
003300 coroner's jury."
003301 
003302 "It was a confession," I ejaculated.
003303 
003304 "No, for it was followed by a protestation of innocence."
003305 
003306 "Coming on the top of such a damning series of events, it was at
003307 least a most suspicious remark."
003308 
003309 "On the contrary," said Holmes, "it is the brightest rift which I
003310 can at present see in the clouds. However innocent he might be,
003311 he could not be such an absolute imbecile as not to see that the
003312 circumstances were very black against him. Had he appeared
003313 surprised at his own arrest, or feigned indignation at it, I
003314 should have looked upon it as highly suspicious, because such
003315 surprise or anger would not be natural under the circumstances,
003316 and yet might appear to be the best policy to a scheming man. His
003317 frank acceptance of the situation marks him as either an innocent
003318 man, or else as a man of considerable self-restraint and
003319 firmness. As to his remark about his deserts, it was also not
003320 unnatural if you consider that he stood beside the dead body of
003321 his father, and that there is no doubt that he had that very day
003322 so far forgotten his filial duty as to bandy words with him, and
003323 even, according to the little girl whose evidence is so
003324 important, to raise his hand as if to strike him. The
003325 self-reproach and contrition which are displayed in his remark
003326 appear to me to be the signs of a healthy mind rather than of a
003327 guilty one."
003328 
003329 I shook my head. "Many men have been hanged on far slighter
003330 evidence," I remarked.
003331 
003332 "So they have. And many men have been wrongfully hanged."
003333 
003334 "What is the young man's own account of the matter?"
003335 
003336 "It is, I am afraid, not very encouraging to his supporters,
003337 though there are one or two points in it which are suggestive.
003338 You will find it here, and may read it for yourself."
003339 
003340 He picked out from his bundle a copy of the local Herefordshire
003341 paper, and having turned down the sheet he pointed out the
003342 paragraph in which the unfortunate young man had given his own
003343 statement of what had occurred. I settled myself down in the
003344 corner of the carriage and read it very carefully. It ran in this
003345 way:
003346 
003347 "Mr. James McCarthy, the only son of the deceased, was then called
003348 and gave evidence as follows: 'I had been away from home for
003349 three days at Bristol, and had only just returned upon the
003350 morning of last Monday, the 3rd. My father was absent from home at
003351 the time of my arrival, and I was informed by the maid that he
003352 had driven over to Ross with John Cobb, the groom. Shortly after
003353 my return I heard the wheels of his trap in the yard, and,
003354 looking out of my window, I saw him get out and walk rapidly out
003355 of the yard, though I was not aware in which direction he was
003356 going. I then took my gun and strolled out in the direction of
003357 the Boscombe Pool, with the intention of visiting the rabbit
003358 warren which is upon the other side. On my way I saw William
003359 Crowder, the game-keeper, as he had stated in his evidence; but
003360 he is mistaken in thinking that I was following my father. I had
003361 no idea that he was in front of me. When about a hundred yards
003362 from the pool I heard a cry of "Cooee!" which was a usual signal
003363 between my father and myself. I then hurried forward, and found
003364 him standing by the pool. He appeared to be much surprised at
003365 seeing me and asked me rather roughly what I was doing there. A
003366 conversation ensued which led to high words and almost to blows,
003367 for my father was a man of a very violent temper. Seeing that his
003368 passion was becoming ungovernable, I left him and returned
003369 towards Hatherley Farm. I had not gone more than 150 yards,
003370 however, when I heard a hideous outcry behind me, which caused me
003371 to run back again. I found my father expiring upon the ground,
003372 with his head terribly injured. I dropped my gun and held him in
003373 my arms, but he almost instantly expired. I knelt beside him for
003374 some minutes, and then made my way to Mr. Turner's lodge-keeper,
003375 his house being the nearest, to ask for assistance. I saw no one
003376 near my father when I returned, and I have no idea how he came by
003377 his injuries. He was not a popular man, being somewhat cold and
003378 forbidding in his manners, but he had, as far as I know, no
003379 active enemies. I know nothing further of the matter.'
003380 
003381 "The Coroner: Did your father make any statement to you before
003382 he died?
003383 
003384 "Witness: He mumbled a few words, but I could only catch some
003385 allusion to a rat.
003386 
003387 "The Coroner: What did you understand by that?
003388 
003389 "Witness: It conveyed no meaning to me. I thought that he was
003390 delirious.
003391 
003392 "The Coroner: What was the point upon which you and your father
003393 had this final quarrel?
003394 
003395 "Witness: I should prefer not to answer.
003396 
003397 "The Coroner: I am afraid that I must press it.
003398 
003399 "Witness: It is really impossible for me to tell you. I can
003400 assure you that it has nothing to do with the sad tragedy which
003401 followed.
003402 
003403 "The Coroner: That is for the court to decide. I need not point
003404 out to you that your refusal to answer will prejudice your case
003405 considerably in any future proceedings which may arise.
003406 
003407 "Witness: I must still refuse.
003408 
003409 "The Coroner: I understand that the cry of 'Cooee' was a common
003410 signal between you and your father?
003411 
003412 "Witness: It was.
003413 
003414 "The Coroner: How was it, then, that he uttered it before he saw
003415 you, and before he even knew that you had returned from Bristol?
003416 
003417 "Witness (with considerable confusion): I do not know.
003418 
003419 "A Juryman: Did you see nothing which aroused your suspicions
003420 when you returned on hearing the cry and found your father
003421 fatally injured?
003422 
003423 "Witness: Nothing definite.
003424 
003425 "The Coroner: What do you mean?
003426 
003427 "Witness: I was so disturbed and excited as I rushed out into
003428 the open, that I could think of nothing except of my father. Yet
003429 I have a vague impression that as I ran forward something lay
003430 upon the ground to the left of me. It seemed to me to be
003431 something grey in colour, a coat of some sort, or a plaid perhaps.
003432 When I rose from my father I looked round for it, but it was
003433 gone.
003434 
003435 "'Do you mean that it disappeared before you went for help?'
003436 
003437 "'Yes, it was gone.'
003438 
003439 "'You cannot say what it was?'
003440 
003441 "'No, I had a feeling something was there.'
003442 
003443 "'How far from the body?'
003444 
003445 "'A dozen yards or so.'
003446 
003447 "'And how far from the edge of the wood?'
003448 
003449 "'About the same.'
003450 
003451 "'Then if it was removed it was while you were within a dozen
003452 yards of it?'
003453 
003454 "'Yes, but with my back towards it.'
003455 
003456 "This concluded the examination of the witness."
003457 
003458 "I see," said I as I glanced down the column, "that the coroner
003459 in his concluding remarks was rather severe upon young McCarthy.
003460 He calls attention, and with reason, to the discrepancy about his
003461 father having signalled to him before seeing him, also to his
003462 refusal to give details of his conversation with his father, and
003463 his singular account of his father's dying words. They are all,
003464 as he remarks, very much against the son."
003465 
003466 Holmes laughed softly to himself and stretched himself out upon
003467 the cushioned seat. "Both you and the coroner have been at some
003468 pains," said he, "to single out the very strongest points in the
003469 young man's favour. Don't you see that you alternately give him
003470 credit for having too much imagination and too little? Too
003471 little, if he could not invent a cause of quarrel which would
003472 give him the sympathy of the jury; too much, if he evolved from
003473 his own inner consciousness anything so outr as a dying
003474 reference to a rat, and the incident of the vanishing cloth. No,
003475 sir, I shall approach this case from the point of view that what
003476 this young man says is true, and we shall see whither that
003477 hypothesis will lead us. And now here is my pocket Petrarch, and
003478 not another word shall I say of this case until we are on the
003479 scene of action. We lunch at Swindon, and I see that we shall be
003480 there in twenty minutes."
003481 
003482 It was nearly four o'clock when we at last, after passing through
003483 the beautiful Stroud Valley, and over the broad gleaming Severn,
003484 found ourselves at the pretty little country-town of Ross. A
003485 lean, ferret-like man, furtive and sly-looking, was waiting for
003486 us upon the platform. In spite of the light brown dustcoat and
003487 leather-leggings which he wore in deference to his rustic
003488 surroundings, I had no difficulty in recognising Lestrade, of
003489 Scotland Yard. With him we drove to the Hereford Arms where a
003490 room had already been engaged for us.
003491 
003492 "I have ordered a carriage," said Lestrade as we sat over a cup
003493 of tea. "I knew your energetic nature, and that you would not be
003494 happy until you had been on the scene of the crime."
003495 
003496 "It was very nice and complimentary of you," Holmes answered. "It
003497 is entirely a question of barometric pressure."
003498 
003499 Lestrade looked startled. "I do not quite follow," he said.
003500 
003501 "How is the glass? Twenty-nine, I see. No wind, and not a cloud
003502 in the sky. I have a caseful of cigarettes here which need
003503 smoking, and the sofa is very much superior to the usual country
003504 hotel abomination. I do not think that it is probable that I
003505 shall use the carriage to-night."
003506 
003507 Lestrade laughed indulgently. "You have, no doubt, already formed
003508 your conclusions from the newspapers," he said. "The case is as
003509 plain as a pikestaff, and the more one goes into it the plainer
003510 it becomes. Still, of course, one can't refuse a lady, and such a
003511 very positive one, too. She has heard of you, and would have your
003512 opinion, though I repeatedly told her that there was nothing
003513 which you could do which I had not already done. Why, bless my
003514 soul! here is her carriage at the door."
003515 
003516 He had hardly spoken before there rushed into the room one of the
003517 most lovely young women that I have ever seen in my life. Her
003518 violet eyes shining, her lips parted, a pink flush upon her
003519 cheeks, all thought of her natural reserve lost in her
003520 overpowering excitement and concern.
003521 
003522 "Oh, Mr. Sherlock Holmes!" she cried, glancing from one to the
003523 other of us, and finally, with a woman's quick intuition,
003524 fastening upon my companion, "I am so glad that you have come. I
003525 have driven down to tell you so. I know that James didn't do it.
003526 I know it, and I want you to start upon your work knowing it,
003527 too. Never let yourself doubt upon that point. We have known each
003528 other since we were little children, and I know his faults as no
003529 one else does; but he is too tender-hearted to hurt a fly. Such a
003530 charge is absurd to anyone who really knows him."
003531 
003532 "I hope we may clear him, Miss Turner," said Sherlock Holmes.
003533 "You may rely upon my doing all that I can."
003534 
003535 "But you have read the evidence. You have formed some conclusion?
003536 Do you not see some loophole, some flaw? Do you not yourself
003537 think that he is innocent?"
003538 
003539 "I think that it is very probable."
003540 
003541 "There, now!" she cried, throwing back her head and looking
003542 defiantly at Lestrade. "You hear! He gives me hopes."
003543 
003544 Lestrade shrugged his shoulders. "I am afraid that my colleague
003545 has been a little quick in forming his conclusions," he said.
003546 
003547 "But he is right. Oh! I know that he is right. James never did
003548 it. And about his quarrel with his father, I am sure that the
003549 reason why he would not speak about it to the coroner was because
003550 I was concerned in it."
003551 
003552 "In what way?" asked Holmes.
003553 
003554 "It is no time for me to hide anything. James and his father had
003555 many disagreements about me. Mr. McCarthy was very anxious that
003556 there should be a marriage between us. James and I have always
003557 loved each other as brother and sister; but of course he is young
003558 and has seen very little of life yet, and--and--well, he
003559 naturally did not wish to do anything like that yet. So there
003560 were quarrels, and this, I am sure, was one of them."
003561 
003562 "And your father?" asked Holmes. "Was he in favour of such a
003563 union?"
003564 
003565 "No, he was averse to it also. No one but Mr. McCarthy was in
003566 favour of it." A quick blush passed over her fresh young face as
003567 Holmes shot one of his keen, questioning glances at her.
003568 
003569 "Thank you for this information," said he. "May I see your father
003570 if I call to-morrow?"
003571 
003572 "I am afraid the doctor won't allow it."
003573 
003574 "The doctor?"
003575 
003576 "Yes, have you not heard? Poor father has never been strong for
003577 years back, but this has broken him down completely. He has taken
003578 to his bed, and Dr. Willows says that he is a wreck and that his
003579 nervous system is shattered. Mr. McCarthy was the only man alive
003580 who had known dad in the old days in Victoria."
003581 
003582 "Ha! In Victoria! That is important."
003583 
003584 "Yes, at the mines."
003585 
003586 "Quite so; at the gold-mines, where, as I understand, Mr. Turner
003587 made his money."
003588 
003589 "Yes, certainly."
003590 
003591 "Thank you, Miss Turner. You have been of material assistance to
003592 me."
003593 
003594 "You will tell me if you have any news to-morrow. No doubt you
003595 will go to the prison to see James. Oh, if you do, Mr. Holmes, do
003596 tell him that I know him to be innocent."
003597 
003598 "I will, Miss Turner."
003599 
003600 "I must go home now, for dad is very ill, and he misses me so if
003601 I leave him. Good-bye, and God help you in your undertaking." She
003602 hurried from the room as impulsively as she had entered, and we
003603 heard the wheels of her carriage rattle off down the street.
003604 
003605 "I am ashamed of you, Holmes," said Lestrade with dignity after a
003606 few minutes' silence. "Why should you raise up hopes which you
003607 are bound to disappoint? I am not over-tender of heart, but I
003608 call it cruel."
003609 
003610 "I think that I see my way to clearing James McCarthy," said
003611 Holmes. "Have you an order to see him in prison?"
003612 
003613 "Yes, but only for you and me."
003614 
003615 "Then I shall reconsider my resolution about going out. We have
003616 still time to take a train to Hereford and see him to-night?"
003617 
003618 "Ample."
003619 
003620 "Then let us do so. Watson, I fear that you will find it very
003621 slow, but I shall only be away a couple of hours."
003622 
003623 I walked down to the station with them, and then wandered through
003624 the streets of the little town, finally returning to the hotel,
003625 where I lay upon the sofa and tried to interest myself in a
003626 yellow-backed novel. The puny plot of the story was so thin,
003627 however, when compared to the deep mystery through which we were
003628 groping, and I found my attention wander so continually from the
003629 action to the fact, that I at last flung it across the room and
003630 gave myself up entirely to a consideration of the events of the
003631 day. Supposing that this unhappy young man's story were
003632 absolutely true, then what hellish thing, what absolutely
003633 unforeseen and extraordinary calamity could have occurred between
003634 the time when he parted from his father, and the moment when,
003635 drawn back by his screams, he rushed into the glade? It was
003636 something terrible and deadly. What could it be? Might not the
003637 nature of the injuries reveal something to my medical instincts?
003638 I rang the bell and called for the weekly county paper, which
003639 contained a verbatim account of the inquest. In the surgeon's
003640 deposition it was stated that the posterior third of the left
003641 parietal bone and the left half of the occipital bone had been
003642 shattered by a heavy blow from a blunt weapon. I marked the spot
003643 upon my own head. Clearly such a blow must have been struck from
003644 behind. That was to some extent in favour of the accused, as when
003645 seen quarrelling he was face to face with his father. Still, it
003646 did not go for very much, for the older man might have turned his
003647 back before the blow fell. Still, it might be worth while to call
003648 Holmes' attention to it. Then there was the peculiar dying
003649 reference to a rat. What could that mean? It could not be
003650 delirium. A man dying from a sudden blow does not commonly become
003651 delirious. No, it was more likely to be an attempt to explain how
003652 he met his fate. But what could it indicate? I cudgelled my
003653 brains to find some possible explanation. And then the incident
003654 of the grey cloth seen by young McCarthy. If that were true the
003655 murderer must have dropped some part of his dress, presumably his
003656 overcoat, in his flight, and must have had the hardihood to
003657 return and to carry it away at the instant when the son was
003658 kneeling with his back turned not a dozen paces off. What a
003659 tissue of mysteries and improbabilities the whole thing was! I
003660 did not wonder at Lestrade's opinion, and yet I had so much faith
003661 in Sherlock Holmes' insight that I could not lose hope as long
003662 as every fresh fact seemed to strengthen his conviction of young
003663 McCarthy's innocence.
003664 
003665 It was late before Sherlock Holmes returned. He came back alone,
003666 for Lestrade was staying in lodgings in the town.
003667 
003668 "The glass still keeps very high," he remarked as he sat down.
003669 "It is of importance that it should not rain before we are able
003670 to go over the ground. On the other hand, a man should be at his
003671 very best and keenest for such nice work as that, and I did not
003672 wish to do it when fagged by a long journey. I have seen young
003673 McCarthy."
003674 
003675 "And what did you learn from him?"
003676 
003677 "Nothing."
003678 
003679 "Could he throw no light?"
003680 
003681 "None at all. I was inclined to think at one time that he knew
003682 who had done it and was screening him or her, but I am convinced
003683 now that he is as puzzled as everyone else. He is not a very
003684 quick-witted youth, though comely to look at and, I should think,
003685 sound at heart."
003686 
003687 "I cannot admire his taste," I remarked, "if it is indeed a fact
003688 that he was averse to a marriage with so charming a young lady as
003689 this Miss Turner."
003690 
003691 "Ah, thereby hangs a rather painful tale. This fellow is madly,
003692 insanely, in love with her, but some two years ago, when he was
003693 only a lad, and before he really knew her, for she had been away
003694 five years at a boarding-school, what does the idiot do but get
003695 into the clutches of a barmaid in Bristol and marry her at a
003696 registry office? No one knows a word of the matter, but you can
003697 imagine how maddening it must be to him to be upbraided for not
003698 doing what he would give his very eyes to do, but what he knows
003699 to be absolutely impossible. It was sheer frenzy of this sort
003700 which made him throw his hands up into the air when his father,
003701 at their last interview, was goading him on to propose to Miss
003702 Turner. On the other hand, he had no means of supporting himself,
003703 and his father, who was by all accounts a very hard man, would
003704 have thrown him over utterly had he known the truth. It was with
003705 his barmaid wife that he had spent the last three days in
003706 Bristol, and his father did not know where he was. Mark that
003707 point. It is of importance. Good has come out of evil, however,
003708 for the barmaid, finding from the papers that he is in serious
003709 trouble and likely to be hanged, has thrown him over utterly and
003710 has written to him to say that she has a husband already in the
003711 Bermuda Dockyard, so that there is really no tie between them. I
003712 think that that bit of news has consoled young McCarthy for all
003713 that he has suffered."
003714 
003715 "But if he is innocent, who has done it?"
003716 
003717 "Ah! who? I would call your attention very particularly to two
003718 points. One is that the murdered man had an appointment with
003719 someone at the pool, and that the someone could not have been his
003720 son, for his son was away, and he did not know when he would
003721 return. The second is that the murdered man was heard to cry
003722 'Cooee!' before he knew that his son had returned. Those are the
003723 crucial points upon which the case depends. And now let us talk
003724 about George Meredith, if you please, and we shall leave all
003725 minor matters until to-morrow."
003726 
003727 There was no rain, as Holmes had foretold, and the morning broke
003728 bright and cloudless. At nine o'clock Lestrade called for us with
003729 the carriage, and we set off for Hatherley Farm and the Boscombe
003730 Pool.
003731 
003732 "There is serious news this morning," Lestrade observed. "It is
003733 said that Mr. Turner, of the Hall, is so ill that his life is
003734 despaired of."
003735 
003736 "An elderly man, I presume?" said Holmes.
003737 
003738 "About sixty; but his constitution has been shattered by his life
003739 abroad, and he has been in failing health for some time. This
003740 business has had a very bad effect upon him. He was an old friend
003741 of McCarthy's, and, I may add, a great benefactor to him, for I
003742 have learned that he gave him Hatherley Farm rent free."
003743 
003744 "Indeed! That is interesting," said Holmes.
003745 
003746 "Oh, yes! In a hundred other ways he has helped him. Everybody
003747 about here speaks of his kindness to him."
003748 
003749 "Really! Does it not strike you as a little singular that this
003750 McCarthy, who appears to have had little of his own, and to have
003751 been under such obligations to Turner, should still talk of
003752 marrying his son to Turner's daughter, who is, presumably,
003753 heiress to the estate, and that in such a very cocksure manner,
003754 as if it were merely a case of a proposal and all else would
003755 follow? It is the more strange, since we know that Turner himself
003756 was averse to the idea. The daughter told us as much. Do you not
003757 deduce something from that?"
003758 
003759 "We have got to the deductions and the inferences," said
003760 Lestrade, winking at me. "I find it hard enough to tackle facts,
003761 Holmes, without flying away after theories and fancies."
003762 
003763 "You are right," said Holmes demurely; "you do find it very hard
003764 to tackle the facts."
003765 
003766 "Anyhow, I have grasped one fact which you seem to find it
003767 difficult to get hold of," replied Lestrade with some warmth.
003768 
003769 "And that is--"
003770 
003771 "That McCarthy senior met his death from McCarthy junior and that
003772 all theories to the contrary are the merest moonshine."
003773 
003774 "Well, moonshine is a brighter thing than fog," said Holmes,
003775 laughing. "But I am very much mistaken if this is not Hatherley
003776 Farm upon the left."
003777 
003778 "Yes, that is it." It was a widespread, comfortable-looking
003779 building, two-storied, slate-roofed, with great yellow blotches
003780 of lichen upon the grey walls. The drawn blinds and the smokeless
003781 chimneys, however, gave it a stricken look, as though the weight
003782 of this horror still lay heavy upon it. We called at the door,
003783 when the maid, at Holmes' request, showed us the boots which her
003784 master wore at the time of his death, and also a pair of the
003785 son's, though not the pair which he had then had. Having measured
003786 these very carefully from seven or eight different points, Holmes
003787 desired to be led to the court-yard, from which we all followed
003788 the winding track which led to Boscombe Pool.
003789 
003790 Sherlock Holmes was transformed when he was hot upon such a scent
003791 as this. Men who had only known the quiet thinker and logician of
003792 Baker Street would have failed to recognise him. His face flushed
003793 and darkened. His brows were drawn into two hard black lines,
003794 while his eyes shone out from beneath them with a steely glitter.
003795 His face was bent downward, his shoulders bowed, his lips
003796 compressed, and the veins stood out like whipcord in his long,
003797 sinewy neck. His nostrils seemed to dilate with a purely animal
003798 lust for the chase, and his mind was so absolutely concentrated
003799 upon the matter before him that a question or remark fell
003800 unheeded upon his ears, or, at the most, only provoked a quick,
003801 impatient snarl in reply. Swiftly and silently he made his way
003802 along the track which ran through the meadows, and so by way of
003803 the woods to the Boscombe Pool. It was damp, marshy ground, as is
003804 all that district, and there were marks of many feet, both upon
003805 the path and amid the short grass which bounded it on either
003806 side. Sometimes Holmes would hurry on, sometimes stop dead, and
003807 once he made quite a little detour into the meadow. Lestrade and
003808 I walked behind him, the detective indifferent and contemptuous,
003809 while I watched my friend with the interest which sprang from the
003810 conviction that every one of his actions was directed towards a
003811 definite end.
003812 
003813 The Boscombe Pool, which is a little reed-girt sheet of water
003814 some fifty yards across, is situated at the boundary between the
003815 Hatherley Farm and the private park of the wealthy Mr. Turner.
003816 Above the woods which lined it upon the farther side we could see
003817 the red, jutting pinnacles which marked the site of the rich
003818 landowner's dwelling. On the Hatherley side of the pool the woods
003819 grew very thick, and there was a narrow belt of sodden grass
003820 twenty paces across between the edge of the trees and the reeds
003821 which lined the lake. Lestrade showed us the exact spot at which
003822 the body had been found, and, indeed, so moist was the ground,
003823 that I could plainly see the traces which had been left by the
003824 fall of the stricken man. To Holmes, as I could see by his eager
003825 face and peering eyes, very many other things were to be read
003826 upon the trampled grass. He ran round, like a dog who is picking
003827 up a scent, and then turned upon my companion.
003828 
003829 "What did you go into the pool for?" he asked.
003830 
003831 "I fished about with a rake. I thought there might be some weapon
003832 or other trace. But how on earth--"
003833 
003834 "Oh, tut, tut! I have no time! That left foot of yours with its
003835 inward twist is all over the place. A mole could trace it, and
003836 there it vanishes among the reeds. Oh, how simple it would all
003837 have been had I been here before they came like a herd of buffalo
003838 and wallowed all over it. Here is where the party with the
003839 lodge-keeper came, and they have covered all tracks for six or
003840 eight feet round the body. But here are three separate tracks of
003841 the same feet." He drew out a lens and lay down upon his
003842 waterproof to have a better view, talking all the time rather to
003843 himself than to us. "These are young McCarthy's feet. Twice he
003844 was walking, and once he ran swiftly, so that the soles are
003845 deeply marked and the heels hardly visible. That bears out his
003846 story. He ran when he saw his father on the ground. Then here are
003847 the father's feet as he paced up and down. What is this, then? It
003848 is the butt-end of the gun as the son stood listening. And this?
003849 Ha, ha! What have we here? Tiptoes! tiptoes! Square, too, quite
003850 unusual boots! They come, they go, they come again--of course
003851 that was for the cloak. Now where did they come from?" He ran up
003852 and down, sometimes losing, sometimes finding the track until we
003853 were well within the edge of the wood and under the shadow of a
003854 great beech, the largest tree in the neighbourhood. Holmes traced
003855 his way to the farther side of this and lay down once more upon
003856 his face with a little cry of satisfaction. For a long time he
003857 remained there, turning over the leaves and dried sticks,
003858 gathering up what seemed to me to be dust into an envelope and
003859 examining with his lens not only the ground but even the bark of
003860 the tree as far as he could reach. A jagged stone was lying among
003861 the moss, and this also he carefully examined and retained. Then
003862 he followed a pathway through the wood until he came to the
003863 highroad, where all traces were lost.
003864 
003865 "It has been a case of considerable interest," he remarked,
003866 returning to his natural manner. "I fancy that this grey house on
003867 the right must be the lodge. I think that I will go in and have a
003868 word with Moran, and perhaps write a little note. Having done
003869 that, we may drive back to our luncheon. You may walk to the cab,
003870 and I shall be with you presently."
003871 
003872 It was about ten minutes before we regained our cab and drove
003873 back into Ross, Holmes still carrying with him the stone which he
003874 had picked up in the wood.
003875 
003876 "This may interest you, Lestrade," he remarked, holding it out.
003877 "The murder was done with it."
003878 
003879 "I see no marks."
003880 
003881 "There are none."
003882 
003883 "How do you know, then?"
003884 
003885 "The grass was growing under it. It had only lain there a few
003886 days. There was no sign of a place whence it had been taken. It
003887 corresponds with the injuries. There is no sign of any other
003888 weapon."
003889 
003890 "And the murderer?"
003891 
003892 "Is a tall man, left-handed, limps with the right leg, wears
003893 thick-soled shooting-boots and a grey cloak, smokes Indian
003894 cigars, uses a cigar-holder, and carries a blunt pen-knife in his
003895 pocket. There are several other indications, but these may be
003896 enough to aid us in our search."
003897 
003898 Lestrade laughed. "I am afraid that I am still a sceptic," he
003899 said. "Theories are all very well, but we have to deal with a
003900 hard-headed British jury."
003901 
003902 "Nous verrons," answered Holmes calmly. "You work your own
003903 method, and I shall work mine. I shall be busy this afternoon,
003904 and shall probably return to London by the evening train."
003905 
003906 "And leave your case unfinished?"
003907 
003908 "No, finished."
003909 
003910 "But the mystery?"
003911 
003912 "It is solved."
003913 
003914 "Who was the criminal, then?"
003915 
003916 "The gentleman I describe."
003917 
003918 "But who is he?"
003919 
003920 "Surely it would not be difficult to find out. This is not such a
003921 populous neighbourhood."
003922 
003923 Lestrade shrugged his shoulders. "I am a practical man," he said,
003924 "and I really cannot undertake to go about the country looking
003925 for a left-handed gentleman with a game leg. I should become the
003926 laughing-stock of Scotland Yard."
003927 
003928 "All right," said Holmes quietly. "I have given you the chance.
003929 Here are your lodgings. Good-bye. I shall drop you a line before
003930 I leave."
003931 
003932 Having left Lestrade at his rooms, we drove to our hotel, where
003933 we found lunch upon the table. Holmes was silent and buried in
003934 thought with a pained expression upon his face, as one who finds
003935 himself in a perplexing position.
003936 
003937 "Look here, Watson," he said when the cloth was cleared "just sit
003938 down in this chair and let me preach to you for a little. I don't
003939 know quite what to do, and I should value your advice. Light a
003940 cigar and let me expound."
003941 
003942  "Pray do so."
003943 
003944 "Well, now, in considering this case there are two points about
003945 young McCarthy's narrative which struck us both instantly,
003946 although they impressed me in his favour and you against him. One
003947 was the fact that his father should, according to his account,
003948 cry 'Cooee!' before seeing him. The other was his singular dying
003949 reference to a rat. He mumbled several words, you understand, but
003950 that was all that caught the son's ear. Now from this double
003951 point our research must commence, and we will begin it by
003952 presuming that what the lad says is absolutely true."
003953 
003954 "What of this 'Cooee!' then?"
003955 
003956 "Well, obviously it could not have been meant for the son. The
003957 son, as far as he knew, was in Bristol. It was mere chance that
003958 he was within earshot. The 'Cooee!' was meant to attract the
003959 attention of whoever it was that he had the appointment with. But
003960 'Cooee' is a distinctly Australian cry, and one which is used
003961 between Australians. There is a strong presumption that the
003962 person whom McCarthy expected to meet him at Boscombe Pool was
003963 someone who had been in Australia."
003964 
003965 "What of the rat, then?"
003966 
003967 Sherlock Holmes took a folded paper from his pocket and flattened
003968 it out on the table. "This is a map of the Colony of Victoria,"
003969 he said. "I wired to Bristol for it last night." He put his hand
003970 over part of the map. "What do you read?"
003971 
003972 "ARAT," I read.
003973 
003974 "And now?" He raised his hand.
003975 
003976 "BALLARAT."
003977 
003978 "Quite so. That was the word the man uttered, and of which his
003979 son only caught the last two syllables. He was trying to utter
003980 the name of his murderer. So and so, of Ballarat."
003981 
003982 "It is wonderful!" I exclaimed.
003983 
003984 "It is obvious. And now, you see, I had narrowed the field down
003985 considerably. The possession of a grey garment was a third point
003986 which, granting the son's statement to be correct, was a
003987 certainty. We have come now out of mere vagueness to the definite
003988 conception of an Australian from Ballarat with a grey cloak."
003989 
003990 "Certainly."
003991 
003992 "And one who was at home in the district, for the pool can only
003993 be approached by the farm or by the estate, where strangers could
003994 hardly wander."
003995 
003996 "Quite so."
003997 
003998 "Then comes our expedition of to-day. By an examination of the
003999 ground I gained the trifling details which I gave to that
004000 imbecile Lestrade, as to the personality of the criminal."
004001 
004002 "But how did you gain them?"
004003 
004004 "You know my method. It is founded upon the observation of
004005 trifles."
004006 
004007 "His height I know that you might roughly judge from the length
004008 of his stride. His boots, too, might be told from their traces."
004009 
004010 "Yes, they were peculiar boots."
004011 
004012 "But his lameness?"
004013 
004014 "The impression of his right foot was always less distinct than
004015 his left. He put less weight upon it. Why? Because he limped--he
004016 was lame."
004017 
004018 "But his left-handedness."
004019 
004020 "You were yourself struck by the nature of the injury as recorded
004021 by the surgeon at the inquest. The blow was struck from
004022 immediately behind, and yet was upon the left side. Now, how can
004023 that be unless it were by a left-handed man? He had stood behind
004024 that tree during the interview between the father and son. He had
004025 even smoked there. I found the ash of a cigar, which my special
004026 knowledge of tobacco ashes enables me to pronounce as an Indian
004027 cigar. I have, as you know, devoted some attention to this, and
004028 written a little monograph on the ashes of 140 different
004029 varieties of pipe, cigar, and cigarette tobacco. Having found the
004030 ash, I then looked round and discovered the stump among the moss
004031 where he had tossed it. It was an Indian cigar, of the variety
004032 which are rolled in Rotterdam."
004033 
004034 "And the cigar-holder?"
004035 
004036 "I could see that the end had not been in his mouth. Therefore he
004037 used a holder. The tip had been cut off, not bitten off, but the
004038 cut was not a clean one, so I deduced a blunt pen-knife."
004039 
004040 "Holmes," I said, "you have drawn a net round this man from which
004041 he cannot escape, and you have saved an innocent human life as
004042 truly as if you had cut the cord which was hanging him. I see the
004043 direction in which all this points. The culprit is--"
004044 
004045 "Mr. John Turner," cried the hotel waiter, opening the door of
004046 our sitting-room, and ushering in a visitor.
004047 
004048 The man who entered was a strange and impressive figure. His
004049 slow, limping step and bowed shoulders gave the appearance of
004050 decrepitude, and yet his hard, deep-lined, craggy features, and
004051 his enormous limbs showed that he was possessed of unusual
004052 strength of body and of character. His tangled beard, grizzled
004053 hair, and outstanding, drooping eyebrows combined to give an air
004054 of dignity and power to his appearance, but his face was of an
004055 ashen white, while his lips and the corners of his nostrils were
004056 tinged with a shade of blue. It was clear to me at a glance that
004057 he was in the grip of some deadly and chronic disease.
004058 
004059 "Pray sit down on the sofa," said Holmes gently. "You had my
004060 note?"
004061 
004062 "Yes, the lodge-keeper brought it up. You said that you wished to
004063 see me here to avoid scandal."
004064 
004065 "I thought people would talk if I went to the Hall."
004066 
004067 "And why did you wish to see me?" He looked across at my
004068 companion with despair in his weary eyes, as though his question
004069 was already answered.
004070 
004071 "Yes," said Holmes, answering the look rather than the words. "It
004072 is so. I know all about McCarthy."
004073 
004074 The old man sank his face in his hands. "God help me!" he cried.
004075 "But I would not have let the young man come to harm. I give you
004076 my word that I would have spoken out if it went against him at
004077 the Assizes."
004078 
004079 "I am glad to hear you say so," said Holmes gravely.
004080 
004081 "I would have spoken now had it not been for my dear girl. It
004082 would break her heart--it will break her heart when she hears
004083 that I am arrested."
004084 
004085 "It may not come to that," said Holmes.
004086 
004087 "What?"
004088 
004089 "I am no official agent. I understand that it was your daughter
004090 who required my presence here, and I am acting in her interests.
004091 Young McCarthy must be got off, however."
004092 
004093 "I am a dying man," said old Turner. "I have had diabetes for
004094 years. My doctor says it is a question whether I shall live a
004095 month. Yet I would rather die under my own roof than in a gaol."
004096 
004097 Holmes rose and sat down at the table with his pen in his hand
004098 and a bundle of paper before him. "Just tell us the truth," he
004099 said. "I shall jot down the facts. You will sign it, and Watson
004100 here can witness it. Then I could produce your confession at the
004101 last extremity to save young McCarthy. I promise you that I shall
004102 not use it unless it is absolutely needed."
004103 
004104 "It's as well," said the old man; "it's a question whether I
004105 shall live to the Assizes, so it matters little to me, but I
004106 should wish to spare Alice the shock. And now I will make the
004107 thing clear to you; it has been a long time in the acting, but
004108 will not take me long to tell.
004109 
004110 "You didn't know this dead man, McCarthy. He was a devil
004111 incarnate. I tell you that. God keep you out of the clutches of
004112 such a man as he. His grip has been upon me these twenty years,
004113 and he has blasted my life. I'll tell you first how I came to be
004114 in his power.
004115 
004116 "It was in the early '60's at the diggings. I was a young chap
004117 then, hot-blooded and reckless, ready to turn my hand at
004118 anything; I got among bad companions, took to drink, had no luck
004119 with my claim, took to the bush, and in a word became what you
004120 would call over here a highway robber. There were six of us, and
004121 we had a wild, free life of it, sticking up a station from time
004122 to time, or stopping the wagons on the road to the diggings.
004123 Black Jack of Ballarat was the name I went under, and our party
004124 is still remembered in the colony as the Ballarat Gang.
004125 
004126 "One day a gold convoy came down from Ballarat to Melbourne, and
004127 we lay in wait for it and attacked it. There were six troopers
004128 and six of us, so it was a close thing, but we emptied four of
004129 their saddles at the first volley. Three of our boys were killed,
004130 however, before we got the swag. I put my pistol to the head of
004131 the wagon-driver, who was this very man McCarthy. I wish to the
004132 Lord that I had shot him then, but I spared him, though I saw his
004133 wicked little eyes fixed on my face, as though to remember every
004134 feature. We got away with the gold, became wealthy men, and made
004135 our way over to England without being suspected. There I parted
004136 from my old pals and determined to settle down to a quiet and
004137 respectable life. I bought this estate, which chanced to be in
004138 the market, and I set myself to do a little good with my money,
004139 to make up for the way in which I had earned it. I married, too,
004140 and though my wife died young she left me my dear little Alice.
004141 Even when she was just a baby her wee hand seemed to lead me down
004142 the right path as nothing else had ever done. In a word, I turned
004143 over a new leaf and did my best to make up for the past. All was
004144 going well when McCarthy laid his grip upon me.
004145 
004146 "I had gone up to town about an investment, and I met him in
004147 Regent Street with hardly a coat to his back or a boot to his
004148 foot.
004149 
004150 "'Here we are, Jack,' says he, touching me on the arm; 'we'll be
004151 as good as a family to you. There's two of us, me and my son, and
004152 you can have the keeping of us. If you don't--it's a fine,
004153 law-abiding country is England, and there's always a policeman
004154 within hail.'
004155 
004156 "Well, down they came to the west country, there was no shaking
004157 them off, and there they have lived rent free on my best land
004158 ever since. There was no rest for me, no peace, no forgetfulness;
004159 turn where I would, there was his cunning, grinning face at my
004160 elbow. It grew worse as Alice grew up, for he soon saw I was more
004161 afraid of her knowing my past than of the police. Whatever he
004162 wanted he must have, and whatever it was I gave him without
004163 question, land, money, houses, until at last he asked a thing
004164 which I could not give. He asked for Alice.
004165 
004166 "His son, you see, had grown up, and so had my girl, and as I was
004167 known to be in weak health, it seemed a fine stroke to him that
004168 his lad should step into the whole property. But there I was
004169 firm. I would not have his cursed stock mixed with mine; not that
004170 I had any dislike to the lad, but his blood was in him, and that
004171 was enough. I stood firm. McCarthy threatened. I braved him to do
004172 his worst. We were to meet at the pool midway between our houses
004173 to talk it over.
004174 
004175 "When I went down there I found him talking with his son, so I
004176 smoked a cigar and waited behind a tree until he should be alone.
004177 But as I listened to his talk all that was black and bitter in
004178 me seemed to come uppermost. He was urging his son to marry my
004179 daughter with as little regard for what she might think as if she
004180 were a slut from off the streets. It drove me mad to think that I
004181 and all that I held most dear should be in the power of such a
004182 man as this. Could I not snap the bond? I was already a dying and
004183 a desperate man. Though clear of mind and fairly strong of limb,
004184 I knew that my own fate was sealed. But my memory and my girl!
004185 Both could be saved if I could but silence that foul tongue. I
004186 did it, Mr. Holmes. I would do it again. Deeply as I have sinned,
004187 I have led a life of martyrdom to atone for it. But that my girl
004188 should be entangled in the same meshes which held me was more
004189 than I could suffer. I struck him down with no more compunction
004190 than if he had been some foul and venomous beast. His cry brought
004191 back his son; but I had gained the cover of the wood, though I
004192 was forced to go back to fetch the cloak which I had dropped in
004193 my flight. That is the true story, gentlemen, of all that
004194 occurred."
004195 
004196 "Well, it is not for me to judge you," said Holmes as the old man
004197 signed the statement which had been drawn out. "I pray that we
004198 may never be exposed to such a temptation."
004199 
004200 "I pray not, sir. And what do you intend to do?"
004201 
004202 "In view of your health, nothing. You are yourself aware that you
004203 will soon have to answer for your deed at a higher court than the
004204 Assizes. I will keep your confession, and if McCarthy is
004205 condemned I shall be forced to use it. If not, it shall never be
004206 seen by mortal eye; and your secret, whether you be alive or
004207 dead, shall be safe with us."
004208 
004209 "Farewell, then," said the old man solemnly. "Your own deathbeds,
004210 when they come, will be the easier for the thought of the peace
004211 which you have given to mine." Tottering and shaking in all his
004212 giant frame, he stumbled slowly from the room.
004213 
004214 "God help us!" said Holmes after a long silence. "Why does fate
004215 play such tricks with poor, helpless worms? I never hear of such
004216 a case as this that I do not think of Baxter's words, and say,
004217 'There, but for the grace of God, goes Sherlock Holmes.'"
004218 
004219 James McCarthy was acquitted at the Assizes on the strength of a
004220 number of objections which had been drawn out by Holmes and
004221 submitted to the defending counsel. Old Turner lived for seven
004222 months after our interview, but he is now dead; and there is
004223 every prospect that the son and daughter may come to live happily
004224 together in ignorance of the black cloud which rests upon their
004225 past.
004226 
004227 
004228 
004229 ADVENTURE V. THE FIVE ORANGE PIPS
004230 
004231 When I glance over my notes and records of the Sherlock Holmes
004232 cases between the years '82 and '90, I am faced by so many which
004233 present strange and interesting features that it is no easy
004234 matter to know which to choose and which to leave. Some, however,
004235 have already gained publicity through the papers, and others have
004236 not offered a field for those peculiar qualities which my friend
004237 possessed in so high a degree, and which it is the object of
004238 these papers to illustrate. Some, too, have baffled his
004239 analytical skill, and would be, as narratives, beginnings without
004240 an ending, while others have been but partially cleared up, and
004241 have their explanations founded rather upon conjecture and
004242 surmise than on that absolute logical proof which was so dear to
004243 him. There is, however, one of these last which was so remarkable
004244 in its details and so startling in its results that I am tempted
004245 to give some account of it in spite of the fact that there are
004246 points in connection with it which never have been, and probably
004247 never will be, entirely cleared up.
004248 
004249 The year '87 furnished us with a long series of cases of greater
004250 or less interest, of which I retain the records. Among my
004251 headings under this one twelve months I find an account of the
004252 adventure of the Paradol Chamber, of the Amateur Mendicant
004253 Society, who held a luxurious club in the lower vault of a
004254 furniture warehouse, of the facts connected with the loss of the
004255 British barque "Sophy Anderson", of the singular adventures of the
004256 Grice Patersons in the island of Uffa, and finally of the
004257 Camberwell poisoning case. In the latter, as may be remembered,
004258 Sherlock Holmes was able, by winding up the dead man's watch, to
004259 prove that it had been wound up two hours before, and that
004260 therefore the deceased had gone to bed within that time--a
004261 deduction which was of the greatest importance in clearing up the
004262 case. All these I may sketch out at some future date, but none of
004263 them present such singular features as the strange train of
004264 circumstances which I have now taken up my pen to describe.
004265 
004266 It was in the latter days of September, and the equinoctial gales
004267 had set in with exceptional violence. All day the wind had
004268 screamed and the rain had beaten against the windows, so that
004269 even here in the heart of great, hand-made London we were forced
004270 to raise our minds for the instant from the routine of life and
004271 to recognise the presence of those great elemental forces which
004272 shriek at mankind through the bars of his civilisation, like
004273 untamed beasts in a cage. As evening drew in, the storm grew
004274 higher and louder, and the wind cried and sobbed like a child in
004275 the chimney. Sherlock Holmes sat moodily at one side of the
004276 fireplace cross-indexing his records of crime, while I at the
004277 other was deep in one of Clark Russell's fine sea-stories until
004278 the howl of the gale from without seemed to blend with the text,
004279 and the splash of the rain to lengthen out into the long swash of
004280 the sea waves. My wife was on a visit to her mother's, and for a
004281 few days I was a dweller once more in my old quarters at Baker
004282 Street.
004283 
004284 "Why," said I, glancing up at my companion, "that was surely the
004285 bell. Who could come to-night? Some friend of yours, perhaps?"
004286 
004287 "Except yourself I have none," he answered. "I do not encourage
004288 visitors."
004289 
004290 "A client, then?"
004291 
004292 "If so, it is a serious case. Nothing less would bring a man out
004293 on such a day and at such an hour. But I take it that it is more
004294 likely to be some crony of the landlady's."
004295 
004296 Sherlock Holmes was wrong in his conjecture, however, for there
004297 came a step in the passage and a tapping at the door. He
004298 stretched out his long arm to turn the lamp away from himself and
004299 towards the vacant chair upon which a newcomer must sit.
004300 
004301 "Come in!" said he.
004302 
004303 The man who entered was young, some two-and-twenty at the
004304 outside, well-groomed and trimly clad, with something of
004305 refinement and delicacy in his bearing. The streaming umbrella
004306 which he held in his hand, and his long shining waterproof told
004307 of the fierce weather through which he had come. He looked about
004308 him anxiously in the glare of the lamp, and I could see that his
004309 face was pale and his eyes heavy, like those of a man who is
004310 weighed down with some great anxiety.
004311 
004312 "I owe you an apology," he said, raising his golden pince-nez to
004313 his eyes. "I trust that I am not intruding. I fear that I have
004314 brought some traces of the storm and rain into your snug
004315 chamber."
004316 
004317 "Give me your coat and umbrella," said Holmes. "They may rest
004318 here on the hook and will be dry presently. You have come up from
004319 the south-west, I see."
004320 
004321 "Yes, from Horsham."
004322 
004323 "That clay and chalk mixture which I see upon your toe caps is
004324 quite distinctive."
004325 
004326 "I have come for advice."
004327 
004328 "That is easily got."
004329 
004330 "And help."
004331 
004332 "That is not always so easy."
004333 
004334 "I have heard of you, Mr. Holmes. I heard from Major Prendergast
004335 how you saved him in the Tankerville Club scandal."
004336 
004337 "Ah, of course. He was wrongfully accused of cheating at cards."
004338 
004339 "He said that you could solve anything."
004340 
004341 "He said too much."
004342 
004343 "That you are never beaten."
004344 
004345 "I have been beaten four times--three times by men, and once by a
004346 woman."
004347 
004348 "But what is that compared with the number of your successes?"
004349 
004350 "It is true that I have been generally successful."
004351 
004352 "Then you may be so with me."
004353 
004354 "I beg that you will draw your chair up to the fire and favour me
004355 with some details as to your case."
004356 
004357 "It is no ordinary one."
004358 
004359 "None of those which come to me are. I am the last court of
004360 appeal."
004361 
004362 "And yet I question, sir, whether, in all your experience, you
004363 have ever listened to a more mysterious and inexplicable chain of
004364 events than those which have happened in my own family."
004365 
004366 "You fill me with interest," said Holmes. "Pray give us the
004367 essential facts from the commencement, and I can afterwards
004368 question you as to those details which seem to me to be most
004369 important."
004370 
004371 The young man pulled his chair up and pushed his wet feet out
004372 towards the blaze.
004373 
004374 "My name," said he, "is John Openshaw, but my own affairs have,
004375 as far as I can understand, little to do with this awful
004376 business. It is a hereditary matter; so in order to give you an
004377 idea of the facts, I must go back to the commencement of the
004378 affair.
004379 
004380 "You must know that my grandfather had two sons--my uncle Elias
004381 and my father Joseph. My father had a small factory at Coventry,
004382 which he enlarged at the time of the invention of bicycling. He
004383 was a patentee of the Openshaw unbreakable tire, and his business
004384 met with such success that he was able to sell it and to retire
004385 upon a handsome competence.
004386 
004387 "My uncle Elias emigrated to America when he was a young man and
004388 became a planter in Florida, where he was reported to have done
004389 very well. At the time of the war he fought in Jackson's army,
004390 and afterwards under Hood, where he rose to be a colonel. When
004391 Lee laid down his arms my uncle returned to his plantation, where
004392 he remained for three or four years. About 1869 or 1870 he came
004393 back to Europe and took a small estate in Sussex, near Horsham.
004394 He had made a very considerable fortune in the States, and his
004395 reason for leaving them was his aversion to the negroes, and his
004396 dislike of the Republican policy in extending the franchise to
004397 them. He was a singular man, fierce and quick-tempered, very
004398 foul-mouthed when he was angry, and of a most retiring
004399 disposition. During all the years that he lived at Horsham, I
004400 doubt if ever he set foot in the town. He had a garden and two or
004401 three fields round his house, and there he would take his
004402 exercise, though very often for weeks on end he would never leave
004403 his room. He drank a great deal of brandy and smoked very
004404 heavily, but he would see no society and did not want any
004405 friends, not even his own brother.
004406 
004407 "He didn't mind me; in fact, he took a fancy to me, for at the
004408 time when he saw me first I was a youngster of twelve or so. This
004409 would be in the year 1878, after he had been eight or nine years
004410 in England. He begged my father to let me live with him and he
004411 was very kind to me in his way. When he was sober he used to be
004412 fond of playing backgammon and draughts with me, and he would
004413 make me his representative both with the servants and with the
004414 tradespeople, so that by the time that I was sixteen I was quite
004415 master of the house. I kept all the keys and could go where I
004416 liked and do what I liked, so long as I did not disturb him in
004417 his privacy. There was one singular exception, however, for he
004418 had a single room, a lumber-room up among the attics, which was
004419 invariably locked, and which he would never permit either me or
004420 anyone else to enter. With a boy's curiosity I have peeped
004421 through the keyhole, but I was never able to see more than such a
004422 collection of old trunks and bundles as would be expected in such
004423 a room.
004424 
004425 "One day--it was in March, 1883--a letter with a foreign stamp
004426 lay upon the table in front of the colonel's plate. It was not a
004427 common thing for him to receive letters, for his bills were all
004428 paid in ready money, and he had no friends of any sort. 'From
004429 India!' said he as he took it up, 'Pondicherry postmark! What can
004430 this be?' Opening it hurriedly, out there jumped five little
004431 dried orange pips, which pattered down upon his plate. I began to
004432 laugh at this, but the laugh was struck from my lips at the sight
004433 of his face. His lip had fallen, his eyes were protruding, his
004434 skin the colour of putty, and he glared at the envelope which he
004435 still held in his trembling hand, 'K. K. K.!' he shrieked, and
004436 then, 'My God, my God, my sins have overtaken me!'
004437 
004438 "'What is it, uncle?' I cried.
004439 
004440 "'Death,' said he, and rising from the table he retired to his
004441 room, leaving me palpitating with horror. I took up the envelope
004442 and saw scrawled in red ink upon the inner flap, just above the
004443 gum, the letter K three times repeated. There was nothing else
004444 save the five dried pips. What could be the reason of his
004445 overpowering terror? I left the breakfast-table, and as I
004446 ascended the stair I met him coming down with an old rusty key,
004447 which must have belonged to the attic, in one hand, and a small
004448 brass box, like a cashbox, in the other.
004449 
004450 "'They may do what they like, but I'll checkmate them still,'
004451 said he with an oath. 'Tell Mary that I shall want a fire in my
004452 room to-day, and send down to Fordham, the Horsham lawyer.'
004453 
004454 "I did as he ordered, and when the lawyer arrived I was asked to
004455 step up to the room. The fire was burning brightly, and in the
004456 grate there was a mass of black, fluffy ashes, as of burned
004457 paper, while the brass box stood open and empty beside it. As I
004458 glanced at the box I noticed, with a start, that upon the lid was
004459 printed the treble K which I had read in the morning upon the
004460 envelope.
004461 
004462 "'I wish you, John,' said my uncle, 'to witness my will. I leave
004463 my estate, with all its advantages and all its disadvantages, to
004464 my brother, your father, whence it will, no doubt, descend to
004465 you. If you can enjoy it in peace, well and good! If you find you
004466 cannot, take my advice, my boy, and leave it to your deadliest
004467 enemy. I am sorry to give you such a two-edged thing, but I can't
004468 say what turn things are going to take. Kindly sign the paper
004469 where Mr. Fordham shows you.'
004470 
004471 "I signed the paper as directed, and the lawyer took it away with
004472 him. The singular incident made, as you may think, the deepest
004473 impression upon me, and I pondered over it and turned it every
004474 way in my mind without being able to make anything of it. Yet I
004475 could not shake off the vague feeling of dread which it left
004476 behind, though the sensation grew less keen as the weeks passed
004477 and nothing happened to disturb the usual routine of our lives. I
004478 could see a change in my uncle, however. He drank more than ever,
004479 and he was less inclined for any sort of society. Most of his
004480 time he would spend in his room, with the door locked upon the
004481 inside, but sometimes he would emerge in a sort of drunken frenzy
004482 and would burst out of the house and tear about the garden with a
004483 revolver in his hand, screaming out that he was afraid of no man,
004484 and that he was not to be cooped up, like a sheep in a pen, by
004485 man or devil. When these hot fits were over, however, he would
004486 rush tumultuously in at the door and lock and bar it behind him,
004487 like a man who can brazen it out no longer against the terror
004488 which lies at the roots of his soul. At such times I have seen
004489 his face, even on a cold day, glisten with moisture, as though it
004490 were new raised from a basin.
004491 
004492 "Well, to come to an end of the matter, Mr. Holmes, and not to
004493 abuse your patience, there came a night when he made one of those
004494 drunken sallies from which he never came back. We found him, when
004495 we went to search for him, face downward in a little
004496 green-scummed pool, which lay at the foot of the garden. There
004497 was no sign of any violence, and the water was but two feet deep,
004498 so that the jury, having regard to his known eccentricity,
004499 brought in a verdict of 'suicide.' But I, who knew how he winced
004500 from the very thought of death, had much ado to persuade myself
004501 that he had gone out of his way to meet it. The matter passed,
004502 however, and my father entered into possession of the estate, and
004503 of some 14,000 pounds, which lay to his credit at the bank."
004504 
004505 "One moment," Holmes interposed, "your statement is, I foresee,
004506 one of the most remarkable to which I have ever listened. Let me
004507 have the date of the reception by your uncle of the letter, and
004508 the date of his supposed suicide."
004509 
004510 "The letter arrived on March 10, 1883. His death was seven weeks
004511 later, upon the night of May 2nd."
004512 
004513 "Thank you. Pray proceed."
004514 
004515 "When my father took over the Horsham property, he, at my
004516 request, made a careful examination of the attic, which had been
004517 always locked up. We found the brass box there, although its
004518 contents had been destroyed. On the inside of the cover was a
004519 paper label, with the initials of K. K. K. repeated upon it, and
004520 'Letters, memoranda, receipts, and a register' written beneath.
004521 These, we presume, indicated the nature of the papers which had
004522 been destroyed by Colonel Openshaw. For the rest, there was
004523 nothing of much importance in the attic save a great many
004524 scattered papers and note-books bearing upon my uncle's life in
004525 America. Some of them were of the war time and showed that he had
004526 done his duty well and had borne the repute of a brave soldier.
004527 Others were of a date during the reconstruction of the Southern
004528 states, and were mostly concerned with politics, for he had
004529 evidently taken a strong part in opposing the carpet-bag
004530 politicians who had been sent down from the North.
004531 
004532 "Well, it was the beginning of '84 when my father came to live at
004533 Horsham, and all went as well as possible with us until the
004534 January of '85. On the fourth day after the new year I heard my
004535 father give a sharp cry of surprise as we sat together at the
004536 breakfast-table. There he was, sitting with a newly opened
004537 envelope in one hand and five dried orange pips in the
004538 outstretched palm of the other one. He had always laughed at what
004539 he called my cock-and-bull story about the colonel, but he looked
004540 very scared and puzzled now that the same thing had come upon
004541 himself.
004542 
004543 "'Why, what on earth does this mean, John?' he stammered.
004544 
004545 "My heart had turned to lead. 'It is K. K. K.,' said I.
004546 
004547 "He looked inside the envelope. 'So it is,' he cried. 'Here are
004548 the very letters. But what is this written above them?'
004549 
004550 "'Put the papers on the sundial,' I read, peeping over his
004551 shoulder.
004552 
004553 "'What papers? What sundial?' he asked.
004554 
004555 "'The sundial in the garden. There is no other,' said I; 'but the
004556 papers must be those that are destroyed.'
004557 
004558 "'Pooh!' said he, gripping hard at his courage. 'We are in a
004559 civilised land here, and we can't have tomfoolery of this kind.
004560 Where does the thing come from?'
004561 
004562 "'From Dundee,' I answered, glancing at the postmark.
004563 
004564 "'Some preposterous practical joke,' said he. 'What have I to do
004565 with sundials and papers? I shall take no notice of such
004566 nonsense.'
004567 
004568 "'I should certainly speak to the police,' I said.
004569 
004570 "'And be laughed at for my pains. Nothing of the sort.'
004571 
004572 "'Then let me do so?'
004573 
004574 "'No, I forbid you. I won't have a fuss made about such
004575 nonsense.'
004576 
004577 "It was in vain to argue with him, for he was a very obstinate
004578 man. I went about, however, with a heart which was full of
004579 forebodings.
004580 
004581 "On the third day after the coming of the letter my father went
004582 from home to visit an old friend of his, Major Freebody, who is
004583 in command of one of the forts upon Portsdown Hill. I was glad
004584 that he should go, for it seemed to me that he was farther from
004585 danger when he was away from home. In that, however, I was in
004586 error. Upon the second day of his absence I received a telegram
004587 from the major, imploring me to come at once. My father had
004588 fallen over one of the deep chalk-pits which abound in the
004589 neighbourhood, and was lying senseless, with a shattered skull. I
004590 hurried to him, but he passed away without having ever recovered
004591 his consciousness. He had, as it appears, been returning from
004592 Fareham in the twilight, and as the country was unknown to him,
004593 and the chalk-pit unfenced, the jury had no hesitation in
004594 bringing in a verdict of 'death from accidental causes.'
004595 Carefully as I examined every fact connected with his death, I
004596 was unable to find anything which could suggest the idea of
004597 murder. There were no signs of violence, no footmarks, no
004598 robbery, no record of strangers having been seen upon the roads.
004599 And yet I need not tell you that my mind was far from at ease,
004600 and that I was well-nigh certain that some foul plot had been
004601 woven round him.
004602 
004603 "In this sinister way I came into my inheritance. You will ask me
004604 why I did not dispose of it? I answer, because I was well
004605 convinced that our troubles were in some way dependent upon an
004606 incident in my uncle's life, and that the danger would be as
004607 pressing in one house as in another.
004608 
004609 "It was in January, '85, that my poor father met his end, and two
004610 years and eight months have elapsed since then. During that time
004611 I have lived happily at Horsham, and I had begun to hope that
004612 this curse had passed away from the family, and that it had ended
004613 with the last generation. I had begun to take comfort too soon,
004614 however; yesterday morning the blow fell in the very shape in
004615 which it had come upon my father."
004616 
004617 The young man took from his waistcoat a crumpled envelope, and
004618 turning to the table he shook out upon it five little dried
004619 orange pips.
004620 
004621 "This is the envelope," he continued. "The postmark is
004622 London--eastern division. Within are the very words which were
004623 upon my father's last message: 'K. K. K.'; and then 'Put the
004624 papers on the sundial.'"
004625 
004626 "What have you done?" asked Holmes.
004627 
004628 "Nothing."
004629 
004630 "Nothing?"
004631 
004632 "To tell the truth"--he sank his face into his thin, white
004633 hands--"I have felt helpless. I have felt like one of those poor
004634 rabbits when the snake is writhing towards it. I seem to be in
004635 the grasp of some resistless, inexorable evil, which no foresight
004636 and no precautions can guard against."
004637 
004638 "Tut! tut!" cried Sherlock Holmes. "You must act, man, or you are
004639 lost. Nothing but energy can save you. This is no time for
004640 despair."
004641 
004642 "I have seen the police."
004643 
004644 "Ah!"
004645 
004646 "But they listened to my story with a smile. I am convinced that
004647 the inspector has formed the opinion that the letters are all
004648 practical jokes, and that the deaths of my relations were really
004649 accidents, as the jury stated, and were not to be connected with
004650 the warnings."
004651 
004652 Holmes shook his clenched hands in the air. "Incredible
004653 imbecility!" he cried.
004654 
004655 "They have, however, allowed me a policeman, who may remain in
004656 the house with me."
004657 
004658 "Has he come with you to-night?"
004659 
004660 "No. His orders were to stay in the house."
004661 
004662 Again Holmes raved in the air.
004663 
004664 "Why did you come to me," he cried, "and, above all, why did you
004665 not come at once?"
004666 
004667 "I did not know. It was only to-day that I spoke to Major
004668 Prendergast about my troubles and was advised by him to come to
004669 you."
004670 
004671 "It is really two days since you had the letter. We should have
004672 acted before this. You have no further evidence, I suppose, than
004673 that which you have placed before us--no suggestive detail which
004674 might help us?"
004675 
004676 "There is one thing," said John Openshaw. He rummaged in his coat
004677 pocket, and, drawing out a piece of discoloured, blue-tinted
004678 paper, he laid it out upon the table. "I have some remembrance,"
004679 said he, "that on the day when my uncle burned the papers I
004680 observed that the small, unburned margins which lay amid the
004681 ashes were of this particular colour. I found this single sheet
004682 upon the floor of his room, and I am inclined to think that it
004683 may be one of the papers which has, perhaps, fluttered out from
004684 among the others, and in that way has escaped destruction. Beyond
004685 the mention of pips, I do not see that it helps us much. I think
004686 myself that it is a page from some private diary. The writing is
004687 undoubtedly my uncle's."
004688 
004689 Holmes moved the lamp, and we both bent over the sheet of paper,
004690 which showed by its ragged edge that it had indeed been torn from
004691 a book. It was headed, "March, 1869," and beneath were the
004692 following enigmatical notices:
004693 
004694 "4th. Hudson came. Same old platform.
004695 
004696 "7th. Set the pips on McCauley, Paramore, and
004697       John Swain, of St. Augustine.
004698 
004699 "9th. McCauley cleared.
004700 
004701 "10th. John Swain cleared.
004702 
004703 "12th. Visited Paramore. All well."
004704 
004705 "Thank you!" said Holmes, folding up the paper and returning it
004706 to our visitor. "And now you must on no account lose another
004707 instant. We cannot spare time even to discuss what you have told
004708 me. You must get home instantly and act."
004709 
004710 "What shall I do?"
004711 
004712 "There is but one thing to do. It must be done at once. You must
004713 put this piece of paper which you have shown us into the brass
004714 box which you have described. You must also put in a note to say
004715 that all the other papers were burned by your uncle, and that
004716 this is the only one which remains. You must assert that in such
004717 words as will carry conviction with them. Having done this, you
004718 must at once put the box out upon the sundial, as directed. Do
004719 you understand?"
004720 
004721 "Entirely."
004722 
004723 "Do not think of revenge, or anything of the sort, at present. I
004724 think that we may gain that by means of the law; but we have our
